Once there, Maul and Death Watch eliminated the battle droids defending the [cyborg](/wiki/Cyborg "Cyborg") general, and Maul then subdued Grievous and gave him a choice: disable the signal powering the droids on the surface, or die. Grievous begrudgingly disabled the signal and was taken into custody. Dooku, who engaged and killed the Nightbrothers in battle, was captured by Shadow Collective forces on the surface, while the disabled battle droids were eliminated.[[54]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Two-54)

After the battle, Maul contacted Mother Talzin once again to inform her of what had happened on Ord Mantell. Talzin promised Maul that, with Dooku and Grievous in custody, they would capture Sidious as well—and gain their revenge against him.[[54]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Two-54) Maul and his forces cleared off of Ord Mantell, leaving little trace they were there, and made their way to [Vizsla Keep 09](/wiki/Vizsla_Keep_09 "Vizsla Keep 09"), a Mandalorian supply outpost.[[11]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Three-11)

 [![Maul tempts Dooku to join him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Maul_Dooku_Allies_or_Death.png/revision/latest?cb=20140716210410) [![Maul tempts Dooku to join him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Maul_Dooku_Allies_or_Death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140716210410)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Maul_Dooku_Allies_or_Death.png/revision/latest?cb=20140716210410) 

Maul tempts Dooku to join him.

 

From the outpost, Maul contacted Darth Sidious, informing him of the capture of Dooku and Grievous. Claiming that he had no further use for the two, Sidious told Maul to kill them, but the former Sith Lord had other plans. Grievous was locked in the brig, while Maul tempted Dooku to join him. They were both betrayed by Sidious, so Maul suggested that he and Dooku could be natural allies. Dooku did not believe that Sidious could be challenged, and claimed he did not think he should ally with Maul and Mother Talzin, the latter of whom once tried to kill Dooku. Talzin herself appeared using Nightsister magic and told the story of how she was once an ally of Sidious, how she too was betrayed when Sidious took Maul from her, and how Sidious was already seeking to replace the Count.[[11]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Three-11) Neither Talzin nor Maul believed Dooku would sincerely ally with them, and simply wanted to ensure he could be taken to Dathomir.[[55]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Four-55)

As they spoke, a Jedi-led Republic assault team [attacked](/wiki/Assault_on_Vizsla_Keep_09 "Assault on Vizsla Keep 09") the supply outpost. The Jedi, including Kenobi, [Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura "Aayla Secura"), [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), and [Tiplee](/wiki/Tiplee "Tiplee"), had tracked the Shadow Collective from Ord Mantell. With both of their lives at stake, Dooku feigned an alliance with Maul, while Grievous escaped in the chaos using an escape pod. Maul and Dooku engaged the Jedi in a lightsaber duel, which lasted until Kast shot a small explosive towards the Jedi, incapacitating the Jedi and allowing Maul and Dooku to escape.[[11]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Three-11)

#### Failure on Dathomir

:   "*At last, the great deceiver comes to rescue his pawn.*"  
    "*I come to end this farce once and for all.*"
:   ―Maul and Darth Sidious[[55]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Four-55)

Having fled the outpost, Maul and his followers made their way towards Dathomir. While en route, Maul was contacted by Moj and the Pykes, who grew concerned that Maul's vendetta was causing the Shadow Collective's plans to fail. Maul assured them that they would be paid and that Sidious would die, allowing the galaxy to be controlled by the Shadow Collective. To ensure loyalty, Maul ordered Saxon to keep the Pykes and Black Sun in line. He also revealed to Dooku that he knew the Sith Lord was not an ally, and that Sidious had ordered his apprentice to feign allegiance with Maul.[[55]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Four-55)

Once on Dathomir, Maul was greeted by Brother Viscus, who survived his fight with Dooku on Ord Mantell. The Nightbrother told Maul that they were ready for the next step of their plan, so Dooku was taken before Mother Talzin, who appeared before them in a cloud of smoke. She unleashed her magic upon the Sith Lord, using it to draw Dooku's life force so she could physically manifest herself again; Talzin's physical return required a sacrifice, and they had chosen Dooku for that purpose. They were interrupted, by an explosion ripping through the area, and the arrival of Grievous and Sidious. Sidious reminded his former apprentice that there was only one plan that mattered: Sidious'.[[55]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Four-55)

 [![Maul fights Grievous, while Talzin in Dooku's body fights Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/2ndBattleDathomir-SoD-4.png/revision/latest?cb=20240317091317) [![Maul fights Grievous, while Talzin in Dooku's body fights Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/2ndBattleDathomir-SoD-4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240317091317)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/2ndBattleDathomir-SoD-4.png/revision/latest?cb=20240317091317) 

Maul fights Grievous, while Talzin in Dooku's body fights Sidious.

 

The arrival of the Dark Lord and Grievous led to a lightsaber duel, one which Talzin joined after she took control of Count Dooku's body. Talzin fought Sidious while Maul fought the cyborg general, and Sidious quickly gained the advantage over the Dathomir witch. Sidious bombarded Talzin with Force lightning, and the witch released Dooku and appeared in physical form once more. Maul, meanwhile, Force-pushed Grievous out of the opening that the explosion created. Once Sidious attacked her with a barrage of lightning, Maul pleaded with his mother to use his own life force to grow more powerful, but Talzin demanded that he retreat as she held off the Dark Lord's attacks. The witch used her powers to toss Maul from the fray and he was dragged away by Kast and another Death Watch warrior. As they fled, Maul watched as Grievous returned to fatally stab Talzin with his lightsabers.[[55]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Four-55)

Maul fled from Dathomir, which was being [attacked](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Dathomir "Second Battle of Dathomir") by the Separatists. The Shadow Collective, meanwhile, had also been defeated by Separatist forces. In Sidious's [eyes](/wiki/Eye "Eye"), despite Maul's escape, the former Sith Lord had been eliminated as a rival to the future Sith rule of the galaxy.[[55]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Four-55)

#### A new plan

:   "*You are but one small piece moving in this mechanism which I have designed, and yet, when you falter, it jeopardizes everything.*"
:   ―Maul to Marg Krim[[56]](#cite_note-Together_Again-56)

Maul and other parts of his loyal forces would eventually return to Mandalore, where they remained in hiding for a short time. The Pyke Syndicate and Black Sun also eventually rejoined the Shadow Collective.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57) At some point, Maul also forged ties with the criminal organization [Crimson Dawn](/wiki/Crimson_Dawn "Crimson Dawn"), led by [Dryden Vos](/wiki/Dryden_Vos "Dryden Vos"). He continued to rule his operation, one part of which involved the transportation of a large shipment of [spice](/wiki/Spice "Spice") by the Pykes.[[56]](#cite_note-Together_Again-56)

 [![Maul threatens to let Crimson Dawn take over Marg Krim's operation.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/43/MaulThreatensKrim-TA.png/revision/latest?cb=20200628035725) [![Maul threatens to let Crimson Dawn take over Marg Krim's operation.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/43/MaulThreatensKrim-TA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200628035725)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/43/MaulThreatensKrim-TA.png/revision/latest?cb=20200628035725) 

Maul threatens to let Crimson Dawn take over Marg Krim's operation.

 

The Pykes hired [Rafa Martez](/wiki/Rafa_Martez "Rafa Martez") to deliver the spice, but after a heavy ethics debate between Martez and the former Jedi Padawan [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"), Martez's sister, [Trace](/wiki/Trace_Martez "Trace Martez"), dumped the spice into [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace"). With no shipment to deliver, the three were taken into custody by the Pykes on [Oba Diah](/wiki/Oba_Diah "Oba Diah"). Shortly afterward, Maul contacted the new leader of the Pykes, [Marg Krim](/wiki/Marg_Krim "Marg Krim"), via hologram about the lost shipment of spice. Krim attempted to assure Maul that the delay of the spice would not jeopardize his plans. Maul warned Krim of further delays, informing him that every piece of his plan was important and if one part of it faltered, the entire plan could be jeopardized. Krim attempted to defend himself by informing him of the ever-growing interference of the Republic against his shipments: one shipment that had arrived on Coruscant was raided by the Republic the week prior.[[56]](#cite_note-Together_Again-56)

Maul asked if any Jedi were involved, but Krim did not know since none of his men survived, which allowed Maul to come to the conclusion that there were. Just then, Maul noticed something hiding in the pipework surrounding where the meeting was taking place and turned to try to see what it was. After searching for a few [seconds](/wiki/Standard_second "Standard second"), he discovered nothing and, not realizing it was Tano, turned back towards Krim, informing him that he had other things to attend to. Maul warned him that if he caused any more delays, he would allow Crimson Dawn to take over the spice operation. With that warning, Maul ended the transmission.[[56]](#cite_note-Together_Again-56)

#### Siege of Mandalore

:   "*With your help, the Jedi can stop Sidious before it's too late.*"  
    "*Too late for what? The Republic to fall? It already has, and you just can't see it! There is no justice, no law, no order, except for the one that will replace it!*"
:   ―Ahsoka Tano and Maul[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57)

 [![Maul at the time of the Siege of Mandalore](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/FineArtPrints-TheUsurper.png/revision/latest?cb=20230629003107) [![Maul at the time of the Siege of Mandalore](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/FineArtPrints-TheUsurper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230629003107)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/FineArtPrints-TheUsurper.png/revision/latest?cb=20230629003107) 

Maul at the time of the Siege of Mandalore

 

In a dream, Maul foresaw that [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") was the key to Sidious's victory as his future Sith apprentice and thus hoped to lure him and Kenobi to Mandalore: Maul hoped to rob Sidious of his prized disciple and finally achieve his revenge against Kenobi.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57) During the final days of the Clone Wars, and two days after returning to Mandalore, Maul and his forces found themselves under [siege](/wiki/Siege_of_Mandalore "Siege of Mandalore") by [Bo-Katan Kryze](/wiki/Bo-Katan_Kryze "Bo-Katan Kryze")'s [legion](/wiki/Mandalore_resistance "Mandalore resistance") of Mandalorians and a [division](/wiki/332nd_Division "332nd Division") of clone troopers led by the recently promoted [Commander](/wiki/Clone_Commander "Clone Commander") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex") and former Jedi Padawan Ahsoka Tano,[[58]](#cite_note-Old_Friends_Not_Forgotten-58) instead of Skywalker[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57) and Kenobi. Maul heard from [Almec](/wiki/Almec "Almec") and his Mandalorian forces that a Jedi was on Mandalore. Assuming that the Jedi was Kenobi, Maul instructed the Shadow Collective to lay out a trap for "Kenobi." The Shadow Collective led Ahsoka Tano and the [clones](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") through the undercity, where they killed all of the clones, including [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Vaughn](/wiki/Vaughn "Vaughn"). Upon seeing that it was Tano that came to confront him, Maul told her that he was expecting Kenobi and asked why she was on Mandalore.[[58]](#cite_note-Old_Friends_Not_Forgotten-58)

Maul continued, telling Tano that he had hoped Kenobi would have come alongside his "loyal foal," Anakin Skywalker, to which Tano revealed that Kenobi had a more important [engagement](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant"). When Tano asked Maul to surrender, he claimed that it would be pointless, as the Jedi Order and the Republic would soon be reduced to nothing and the galaxy would come under the control of Darth Sidious. Just then, clone forces led by Rex arrived and opened fire, forcing Maul and his Mandalorian forces to flee.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57)

During the ensuing combat, Maul captured and interrogated [ARC trooper](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Commando "Advanced Recon Commando") [Jesse](/wiki/Jesse "Jesse") about Ahsoka's history, but Jesse refused to tell him anything. Maul ordered [Gar Saxon](/wiki/Gar_Saxon "Gar Saxon") to assassinate the captured Almec before he could reveal any vital information to the enemy. Afterward, he focused again on Jesse and eventually managed to make him reveal everything he wanted to know using a [mind probe](/wiki/Mind_probe_(Force_power) "Mind probe (Force power)").[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57)

 [![Maul orders Ziton Moj, Marg Krim, and Dryden Vos to go into hiding.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/SyndicateLeadersGoHide-TPA.png/revision/latest?cb=20200425020800) [![Maul orders Ziton Moj, Marg Krim, and Dryden Vos to go into hiding.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/SyndicateLeadersGoHide-TPA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20200425020800)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/SyndicateLeadersGoHide-TPA.png/revision/latest?cb=20200425020800) 

Maul orders Ziton Moj, Marg Krim, and Dryden Vos to go into hiding.

 

Later, Maul was speaking with Shadow Collective leaders [Marg Krim](/wiki/Marg_Krim "Marg Krim") of the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate"), [Ziton Moj](/wiki/Ziton_Moj "Ziton Moj") of the [Black Sun](/wiki/Black_Sun "Black Sun"), and [Dryden Vos](/wiki/Dryden_Vos "Dryden Vos") of the [Crimson Dawn](/wiki/Crimson_Dawn "Crimson Dawn"), ordering them to go into hiding, when Saxon returned to report the success of his mission. Maul took the time to thank him, [Rook Kast](/wiki/Rook_Kast "Rook Kast"), and the other Mandalorians for saving him weeks prior, and explained to them that the galaxy would be remade soon and that they needed to seize as much power as they could. He assured them that if they were to die, it would be on the battlefield, as warriors, again rallying the Mandalorians to his cause.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57)

Sometime later, Maul returned to the throne room when Ahsoka Tano, Bo-Katan, and Rex entered. Bo-Katan attempted to attack him, but Maul effortlessly waved away her blaster bolts and subdued her before handing Jesse back to them as a show of "good faith." After Tano told Bo-Katan and Rex to leave, Maul was left alone with her. As the battle outside was raging on, Maul began talking in a calm manner to Ahsoka, reminding her of the hypocrisy of the Jedi Order, which caused her to leave, and that they were both tools used by a greater power.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57)

 [![After his offer to work together to destroy Sidious was denied, Maul engaged Ahsoka in a fierce duel that began in the throne room.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/MaulAhsokaClash-TPA.png/revision/latest?cb=20200425014801) [![After his offer to work together to destroy Sidious was denied, Maul engaged Ahsoka in a fierce duel that began in the throne room.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/MaulAhsokaClash-TPA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200425014801)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/MaulAhsokaClash-TPA.png/revision/latest?cb=20200425014801) 

After his offer to work together to destroy Sidious was denied, Maul engaged Ahsoka in a fierce duel that began in the throne room.

 

Maul then told her again that what she called justice would soon be changed along with the entire galaxy, revealing that he was talking about Sidious. Ahsoka suggested that Maul help the Jedi stop Sidious before this would happen, only for Maul to insist that it was already too late, as the Republic was too corrupted to be saved and the Jedi couldn't possibly stop Sidious. Maul then asked Ahsoka to join him, suggesting that together they could defeat Sidious. After a long moment of consideration, Ahsoka agreed on the condition that Maul answer one question: what did he want with Skywalker. He stated that he was the key to everything, to destruction, and that he had a vision which revealed that Sidious sought to make Skywalker his new apprentice.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57)

When Ahsoka accused him of lying, Maul explained that he had engineered the conflict on Mandalore to lure out Kenobi and Skywalker, so that he could kill the latter before he would turn to the Dark Side. Hearing this, Ahsoka changed her mind and ignited her lightsabers, stating that she knew Skywalker and he could never turn. Angered by the rejection, Maul stated that Ahsoka needed one more lesson and activated his own lightsaber. The two [Force-Sensitive Outcasts](/wiki/Force-Sensitive_Outcast "Force-Sensitive Outcast") then engaged in a fierce duel, during which Ahsoka proved to be a very tough opponent for Maul, despite the latter being stronger and far more experienced than her. Maul managed to disarm Ahsoka of her main saber, though she quickly retrieved it with the Force. Ahsoka then taunted Maul, stating he was lucky Anakin had not shown up. Maul compared this to Kenobi's arrogance. The two continued fighting and briefly engaged in a saber lock, with Maul gaining the upper hand, though he was caught by surprise by Ahsoka, who managed to kick him outside through a glass window.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57)

#### Caught and released

:   "*Now, if you will follow my lead—*"  
    "*You don't understand. I'm not here to team up with you. I need a diversion, and you're it. Now go cause some chaos. It's what you're good at.*"  
    "*Uh, care to give me a fighting chance?*"  
    "*I'm not rooting for you. Now get going.*"
:   ―Maul and Ahsoka Tano, after she freed him — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/NotRootingForYou-Shattered.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250327205902)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:NotRootingForYou-Shattered.flac "File:NotRootingForYou-Shattered.flac"))[[59]](#cite_note-Shattered-59)

 [![After disarming Ahsoka, Maul gave her one last chance to join him or die.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/OneFinalTime.png/revision/latest?cb=20200710234635) [![After disarming Ahsoka, Maul gave her one last chance to join him or die.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/OneFinalTime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20200710234635)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/OneFinalTime.png/revision/latest?cb=20200710234635) 

After disarming Ahsoka, Maul gave her one last chance to join him or die.

 

Outside, Ahsoka chased Maul to the top of a building. As his Mandalorian forces were being overrun, Saxon contacted Maul asking for reinforcements, but he abandoned him, saying that a ship would soon be arriving to pick him up. Saxon and his forces were outnumbered by clone troopers and forced to surrender shortly afterward. As Maul reached the top of the building, Ahsoka caught up with him and the two resumed their duel, before Maul's ship arrived to pick him up. Ahsoka stopped him from escaping, only for Maul to disarm her of both her lightsabers and slash the beam she was standing on. With Tano cornered, Maul gave her one last chance to join him, but she refused, causing him to slash at her angrily. Dodging his strikes, Tano grabbed Maul's saber and tripped him over the edge of the beam, though she saved him from falling to his death with the Force.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57)

Preferring to die rather than be captured, Maul told Ahsoka to let him fall, but she refused, just as three [LAAT gunships](/wiki/Low_Altitude_Assault_Transport/infantry "Low Altitude Assault Transport/infantry") arrived. Maul furiously told Ahsoka she had no idea what she had just done and that they were all going to die soon, before being stunned and taken into custody.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57) The Shadow Collective would collapse after Maul's defeat at Mandalore.[[60]](#cite_note-Much_to_Learn_Pykes-60) Maul was subsequently imprisoned within a [Mandalorian vault](/wiki/Mandalorian_vault "Mandalorian vault") designed to restrain Force-users and placed aboard the [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer")[[59]](#cite_note-Shattered-59) *[Tribunal](/wiki/Tribunal "Tribunal")*[[61]](#cite_note-TCW_Character_Encyclopedia-61) commanded by Ahsoka, who was told by the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") to bring him to Coruscant so that he could stand trial for his crimes. [En route](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_the_Tribunal "Skirmish aboard the Tribunal") to Coruscant however, Palpatine (who had revealed himself as Darth Sidious) initiated [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), causing Rex and the rest of Ahsoka's clone troopers to turn on her. Maul sensed these events while in his captivity, before a pair of clones arrived to execute him, having received a different order from Sidious, who wanted to be rid of his former apprentice once and for all.[[59]](#cite_note-Shattered-59)

 [![Maul, restrained within a Mandalorian vault, being escorted by Bo-Katan Kryze, Ursa Wren and other Nite Owls.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/UrsaBoKatanTransportMaul-Shattered.png/revision/latest?cb=20200429010702) [![Maul, restrained within a Mandalorian vault, being escorted by Bo-Katan Kryze, Ursa Wren and other Nite Owls.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/UrsaBoKatanTransportMaul-Shattered.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20200429010702)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/UrsaBoKatanTransportMaul-Shattered.png/revision/latest?cb=20200429010702) 

Maul, restrained within a Mandalorian vault, being escorted by Bo-Katan Kryze, Ursa Wren and other Nite Owls.

 

Before the clones could shoot the renegade Sith Lord, Ahsoka knocked them out and subsequently freed Maul from his restraints. He expressed his surprise that Tano had survived, but she threatened him with her lightsabers and demanded to know if he was behind the events, which the former Sith denied. She then revealed that the clones had turned against her and Maul laughed at the "brilliance" of Sidious' plan to use the Jedi's army to destroy them, much to her disgust. Maul went on to explain that despite being Sidious's apprentice, he was unaware of the plan's finer details. He then proposed a team-up with the former Jedi Padawan, but she harshly rejected his offer and told him he was merely a distraction to cause some chaos, refusing to lend him one of her weapons to aid in his escape. Despite being unarmed, Maul, using the Force to rip panels from the walls, tore a path of destruction through the ship, slaughtering every clone trooper in his way. When a group of clones attempted to seal themselves off from him, he used the Force to pull one of the troopers' arms through the closing [blast door](/wiki/Blast_door "Blast door"), severing it[[59]](#cite_note-Shattered-59) and providing Maul with an active [wrist comm](/wiki/Wrist_comm "Wrist comm") connection to the clones' radio chatter.[[62]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-62)

 [![Maul destroys the hyperdrive with the Force](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/MaulDestroysHyperdrive-VaD.png/revision/latest?cb=20200506064709) [![Maul destroys the hyperdrive with the Force](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/MaulDestroysHyperdrive-VaD.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20200506064709)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/MaulDestroysHyperdrive-VaD.png/revision/latest?cb=20200506064709) 

Maul destroys the hyperdrive with the Force

 

Maul then made his way to the [hyperdrive](/wiki/Hyperdrive "Hyperdrive") room, still using his stolen wrist comm to listen in on the clones. Two troopers then showed up and aimed their guns at him, but he effortlessly lifted them into the air and choked them. Entering the hyperdrive room, Maul quickly dispatched of all the clones using the Force, and tore the control console away before pulling the hyperdrive generators down, causing the vessel to drop out of lightspeed over a [moon](/wiki/Unidentified_moon "Unidentified moon"), where it became caught in its gravity well. As the ship began falling out of the sky and onto the moon's surface, Maul made his way to the [hangar](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar") and began running towards a [shuttle](/wiki/Nu-class_attack/transport_shuttle "Nu-class attack/transport shuttle"). Ahsoka saw him and gave chase, but Maul attacked her with the Force and said that he was only causing chaos as she wanted. Enraged, Ahsoka nearly killed him with a swipe from her lightsabers, but he retaliated by pushing her into a pit, though she was saved by the [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") [RG-G1](/wiki/RG-G1 "RG-G1"). Maul then tried to take off in the shuttle and, though Ahsoka attempted to stop him again and grabbed the shuttle using the Force, she was ultimately forced to let him go when both [R7-A7](/wiki/R7-A7 "R7-A7") and Rex (who had had his [behavioral modification biochip](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") removed by Ahsoka) were shot by clone troopers, allowing Maul to escape into hyperspace,[[62]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-62) planning to rebuild his empire.[[61]](#cite_note-TCW_Character_Encyclopedia-61)

In the [Mustafarian mining facility](/wiki/Klegger_Corp_Mining_Facility "Klegger Corp Mining Facility") on Mustafar, Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker [dueled each other](/wiki/Duel_on_Mustafar "Duel on Mustafar") and made their way into the [war room](/wiki/Separatist_Council_war_room "Separatist Council war room") and momentarily into a nearby [conference room](/wiki/Separatist_Council_Conference_Room "Separatist Council Conference Room"). During the duel with his former apprentice,[[63]](#cite_note-Episode_III-63) feeling his former friend's focused hatred was horrifying, as Kenobi had felt it from Maul, Dooku, Opress, and Ventress.[[64]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-64)

### Age of the Empire

#### A hunted shadow

:   "*Maul, what game are you playing?"  
    "The end game, Lady Tano. The end game. I am the enemy of your enemy now, and I have my own reasons for wanting the Empire to fall. But we have little time. The one they call Vader will be here soon.*"
:   ―Ahsoka Tano and Maul[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

As Maul had foreseen,[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57) Anakin Skywalker did indeed fall to the dark side, becoming Sidious' next apprentice and taking on the name Darth Vader. With his new student at his side, Sidious established the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") and enacted the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge"), the next step in his grand plan.[[63]](#cite_note-Episode_III-63)[[59]](#cite_note-Shattered-59) Vader and the [Jedi-hunting](/wiki/Jedi_hunter "Jedi hunter") [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius") were set loose to eradicate the Order that Maul had once wished to topple.[[65]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_14-65) Maul himself became a target of these [Inquisitors](/wiki/Inquisitor "Inquisitor"), but, for all their skills, they were unsuccessful in discovering his whereabouts. Over the years, Maul remained elusive enough to the Imperial hunters that they began to refer to him as "The Shadow."[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18) In time, Maul acquired a [new lightsaber](/wiki/Maul%27s_lightsaber "Maul's lightsaber"), which appeared as if it used parts salvaged from an [Inquisitor's double-bladed lightsaber](/wiki/Double-bladed_spinning_lightsaber "Double-bladed spinning lightsaber").[[66]](#cite_note-Mini_Book_of_Lightsabers-66)

Following the outbreak of the Jedi Purge, Maul became a subject of interest to the renegade Padawan [Ferren Barr](/wiki/Ferren_Barr "Ferren Barr"), who kept a file on the former Sith Lord within the archives of [Endee](/wiki/Endee "Endee"), an [R1-series astromech droid](/wiki/R1-series_astromech_droid "R1-series astromech droid") under his possession. Barr had gathered information on both Maul as well as several other subjects, hoping to better understand how the Jedi met their downfall so quickly at the hands of the Sith.[[65]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_14-65) During the [Invasion of Mon Cala](/wiki/Invasion_of_Mon_Cala "Invasion of Mon Cala")[[67]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_16-67) in [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"),[[68]](#cite_note-Mon_Cala_Date-68) Barr and [his disciples](/wiki/Ferren_Barr%27s_disciples "Ferren Barr's disciples") were discovered by Vader. The Padawan had Endee upload a backup of the archive to a [datacard](/wiki/Datacard "Datacard") before instructing the droid to self-destruct.[[67]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_16-67) Barr himself died in combat with Vader soon after.[[69]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_17-69)

In [8 BBY](/wiki/8_BBY "8 BBY") or [7 BBY](/wiki/7_BBY "7 BBY"),[[70]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_15_date-70) Kenobi, now hiding on Tatooine, was confronted by [moisture farmer](/wiki/Moisture_farmer "Moisture farmer") [Owen Lars](/wiki/Owen_Lars "Owen Lars"), who warned Kenobi to stay away from his nephew, [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), secretly Anakin Skywalker's son. Lars stated that Kenobi was a dangerous man who could never keep out of trouble. After Lars left his [home](/wiki/Ben_Kenobi%27s_home "Ben Kenobi's home"), Kenobi mentally agreed with Lars before also noting that he had a knack for surviving, recalling his encounters with Maul, Dooku, Grievous, and Jabba.[[71]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_15-71)

#### Leading the Five Crime Syndicates

:   "*But that was when the five syndicates worked against each other. Now that we are allies, we cooperate. I suppose* [Aemon] *misses the good old days, when we could operate however we wanted. It certainly had some benefits. But our current overseer does encourage some independence, as long as we don't go against his rules about infighting and vengeance. His methods for business got enough of us rich that he silenced most of the protestors. And anyone else, well, he had a method for silencing them, too.*"
:   ―Dryden Vos[[13]](#cite_note-Climb-13)

 [![Maul was contacted by Qi'ra after Dryden Vos was killed.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/MaulWantsQiraClose-Solo7.png/revision/latest?cb=20190410005326) [![Maul was contacted by Qi'ra after Dryden Vos was killed.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/MaulWantsQiraClose-Solo7.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20190410005326)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/MaulWantsQiraClose-Solo7.png/revision/latest?cb=20190410005326) 

Maul was contacted by Qi'ra after Dryden Vos was killed.

 

Sometime after his escape during the Purge, Maul had once again returned to Dathomir, where he took up residence,[[14]](#cite_note-Solo-14) frequently haunting the dead world, using Nightsisters' relics, tomes, and specially crafted potions to increase power and advance his desire for vengeance,[[72]](#cite_note-Dawn_of_Rebellion-72) and became the shadowy leader of [Crimson Dawn](/wiki/Crimson_Dawn "Crimson Dawn"), with [Dryden Vos](/wiki/Dryden_Vos "Dryden Vos") as his figurehead.[[14]](#cite_note-Solo-14) Despite the fall of the Shadow Collective,[[60]](#cite_note-Much_to_Learn_Pykes-60) he also had control of the [Five Crime Syndicates](/wiki/Five_Crime_Syndicates "Five Crime Syndicates") and prevented them from fighting with one another. However, not all members of the syndicates were happy with this arrangement, with Black Sun member [Alorium](/wiki/Alorium "Alorium") believing that Maul "[kept] them under his boot". However, the riches reaped from Maul's leadership kept most of his protestors silent, with Maul making sure to silence any detractors who did not keep quiet. Due in part to his desire for independence from Maul, Alorium unsuccessfully attempted to take over a part of the Black Sun organization.[[13]](#cite_note-Climb-13) During his time as leader of Crimson Dawn, Maul began a search for an ancient [Sith holocron](/wiki/Sith_holocron "Sith holocron"). While searching, Maul used a tactic of stealth, wearing a hooded cloak to hide his appearance and exchanged his double-bladed lightsaber for another [one](/wiki/Maul%27s_lightsaber "Maul's lightsaber") which he added a wooden part to in order to give it the appearance of a staff.[[26]](#cite_note-LaJE-26)

In the time after Alorium's failed coup, Vos's underling [Qi'ra](/wiki/Qi%27ra "Qi'ra")[[13]](#cite_note-Climb-13) met Maul for the first time,[[73]](#cite_note-Alex_Tweet-73) with Qi'ra considering the act of meeting him something she could not walk away from and thus set her future in stone.[[13]](#cite_note-Climb-13) In [10 BBY](/wiki/10_BBY "10 BBY"),[[3]](#cite_note-Timelines-3) following Vos's death, Maul was contacted by Qi'ra, who informed him that Vos had been [betrayed and murdered](/wiki/Showdown_on_Savareen "Showdown on Savareen") by [Tobias Beckett](/wiki/Tobias_Beckett "Tobias Beckett") and [his](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") [associates](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca") that he employed, before having his shipment of [coaxium](/wiki/Coaxium "Coaxium") stolen while it was being refined on the desert planet [Savareen](/wiki/Savareen "Savareen").[[14]](#cite_note-Solo-14)

 [![Working more closely with Qi'ra, Maul taught her many secrets of the Sith.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/QiraMaul-CrimsonReign1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250402235438) [![Working more closely with Qi'ra, Maul taught her many secrets of the Sith.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/QiraMaul-CrimsonReign1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20250402235438)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/QiraMaul-CrimsonReign1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250402235438) 

Working more closely with Qi'ra, Maul taught her many secrets of the Sith.

 

Irritated, Maul recalled Qi'ra to Dathomir, where he said that the two would decide how best to deal with Beckett and the other traitors. He then activated his new lightsaber and told Qi'ra that they would be working more closely from then on,[[14]](#cite_note-Solo-14) elevating her to the late Vos's position.[[5]](#cite_note-UltimateStarWarsNewE-5) Maul taught Qi'ra about the Sith Order, revealing to her on his mutterings the Rule of Two, he told her that Galactic Emperor Sheev Palpatine was actually the Dark Lord of the Sith known as Darth Sidious and that the Imperial enforcer Darth Vader was his Sith apprentice. Maul told her about his plan to use Crimson Dawn to take down the Empire.[[74]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_1-74) He also trained Qi'ra to fight the Sith.[[17]](#cite_note-War_of_the_Bounty_Hunters_3-17) Through Qi'ra and the Dawn, Maul's desire for vengeance against the Sith continues as the organization tries to destroy them.[[75]](#cite_note-The_Comprehensive_Guide_to_the_Star_Wars_Galaxy-75)

Maul learned about the [Fermata Cage](/wiki/Fermata_Cage "Fermata Cage"), a [weapon](/wiki/Weapon "Weapon") of the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") which could freeze individual moments and was used to contain an [ancient Sith Lord](/wiki/Unidentified_Sith_Lord_(Fermata_Cage) "Unidentified Sith Lord (Fermata Cage)"). Maul planned to free the Sith Lord and watch them come after both Sidious and Vader in accordance to the Rule of Two. Unfortunately, Maul's attempts were unsuccessful.[[76]](#cite_note-Hidden_Empire_1-76)

#### Faces of the Damanos castle

##### Oppression of the past

:   "*You. Failed. Me.*"
:   ―The voice of Savage Opress, as used used against Maul[[77]](#cite_note-Ghosts-77)

 [![Maul (pictured) traveled across the galaxy in search for ways to destroy Sidious and Kenobi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/13/Maul-BHUSC.png/revision/latest?cb=20221205024356) [![Maul (pictured) traveled across the galaxy in search for ways to destroy Sidious and Kenobi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/13/Maul-BHUSC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221205024356)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/13/Maul-BHUSC.png/revision/latest?cb=20221205024356) 

Maul (pictured) traveled across the galaxy in search for ways to destroy Sidious and Kenobi.

 

During the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), Maul became obsessed with the destruction of Sidious and his revenge on Kenobi. Knowing that he could not underestimate either enemy, he scoured worlds in search of an advantage in his missions.[[28]](#cite_note-TSWB-28) Sometime between [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY") and [5 BBY](/wiki/5_BBY "5 BBY"),[[78]](#cite_note-GhostsDate-78) one of these excursions [brought](/wiki/Mission_to_Damanos "Mission to Damanos") Maul to a [Sith castle](/wiki/Sith_castle "Sith castle") on the ash-gray planet [Damanos](/wiki/Damanos "Damanos")[[77]](#cite_note-Ghosts-77) in the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"),[[79]](#cite_note-Appendix-79) where he would encounter [visions](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision") of unexpected familiar faces. Inside the castle, he first interacted with a vision of Savage Opress, who claimed to reject Maul for neither being his brother nor his master. The vision began to duel Maul, who blocked the powerful, rage-fueled assault until his brother's false specter knocked him down. Maul turned away from him and swung his blade at his "brother's" feet, with "Opress" avoiding the attack with a leap. After circling each other, waiting for the other to strike, Maul told "Opress" he knew what he wanted, and all he wanted was to balance the scales for what they did to him, their mother, and himself.[[77]](#cite_note-Ghosts-77)

"Opress" began to laugh, mocking him and alleging that what truly motivated him now was a desire to no longer feel powerless. Maul's rage grew with each word and attacked, landing atop his brother's fake specter by the time he was finished and crashing his lightsaber into his opponent's. While "Opress" managed to parry Maul's next strike, Maul noticed the weakness in his posture and realized the foe before him was an imposter, not his real brother. Eventually, Maul cornered him, grabbed back of his neck, and pulled him toward him. The fake Opress began to beg, but Maul declared that he was no brother of his and thrust his blade through the imposter's belly, leaving the fake Sith to crumple lifelessly to the ground. Pushing aside the body, Maul looked down for a moment, only to feel there was no reason to. Entertaining that he was confirming his enemy was dead or that he wanted to see his brother's face one last time, he was instead greeted with a vision of his own corpse and a whisper in Opress's voice, alleging that Maul had failed him. An angered Maul stole another glance towards his "corpse" and then continued forward.[[77]](#cite_note-Ghosts-77)

##### A grievous feeling

:   "*I never asked for any of this! You and your masters took everything from me! My family, my power—you left me with nothing!*"  
    "*You didn't ask for this, that much is true, but you never leave it behind.*"
:   ―Maul and the vision of Grievous[[77]](#cite_note-Ghosts-77)

 [![A vision of General Grievous (pictured) attacked Maul](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/AoR-GeneralGrievous-Larraz-textless.png/revision/latest?cb=20190626135036) [![A vision of General Grievous (pictured) attacked Maul](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/AoR-GeneralGrievous-Larraz-textless.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190626135036)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/AoR-GeneralGrievous-Larraz-textless.png/revision/latest?cb=20190626135036) 

A vision of General Grievous (pictured) attacked Maul

 

Maul descended deeper into the castle, entering what he assumed to be its throne room, and began pondering how long it had been since someone had passed through its halls, as well as what life on the world had been like. Maul sensed a powerful energy as he moved further into the castle and encountered a vision of General Grievous waiting for him, pouncing from the ceiling and bearing down with all four of his lightsabers. Narrowing avoiding the general, Maul rolled out of "Grievous's" path and angrily glared at his opponent, to which "Grievous" asked if he remembered their encounter on Dathomir, in which he had slaid Maul's mother, Talzin. Keeping his eyes on the cyborg, he recalled and told him that Kenobi had killed him, to which "Grievous" only mocked him further by asking how it felt for Maul's sworn enemy to steal his revenge. Maul focused on his anger—choosing to ignore another strong emotion emerging inside of him, the pain of his losses—and attacked "Grievous," taking two of the general's hands and lightsabers within them in his offensive before pinning him down. Grievous, however, laughed and recalled Maul's anguished expression after he killed his mother, pondering if that expression would appear when he plunged his lightsabers into him next. Maul responded with a scream in which he declared that the Grievous before him was not real, which the specter admitted to be true. Using that, "Grievous" asked if he felt any comfort in knowing the person who murdered his mother was no longer alive. Seeing it did not as Maul found himself unable to answer, he responded for Maul and kicked, catching him off guard and knocking him back.[[77]](#cite_note-Ghosts-77)

Maul immediately jumped into a defensive position, expecting "Grievous" to attack, but he did not and instead silently stared at him. His anger out of control, Maul raged at the cyborg, recalling how he had no choice in the life he was forced to live, to which "Grievous" responded Maul was refusing to leave that life behind. Maul screamed and lunged at "Grievous," clashing lightsabers with the general's apparition, who parried each hate-filled attack and never went on the offensive himself, something Maul noticed, and thought was odd. Instead, "Grievous" continued to taunt Maul about his lost family and purpose, to which Maul responded by drawing on the anger those words instilled and severing another of "Grievous's" hands, leaving the cyborg with only one remaining lightsaber. Seemingly unharmed by his injuries, "Grievous" asked what else Maul felt and laughed at the former Sith Lord, whose internal darkness, combined with the darkness of the Sith castle, left Maul with a feeling akin to an open wound. Just as he did with his mother, Maul drove his lightsaber through "Grievous," cutting his maniacal delight short. "Grievous" fell silently back into the darkness, vanishing but leaving Maul with no satisfaction, just as the specter had foretold: even after slaying the person who had killed his mother, Maul only felt rage within himself, to which he screamed.[[77]](#cite_note-Ghosts-77)

##### Qui-Gon Jinn's offer

:   "*I'm here to offer you a choice, Maul. I want you to leave this castle, forget that it exists, and take your first step on the path toward a different destiny.*"  
    "*I see. And what path is this—the path of the Jedi?*"  
    "*I thought you were above such narrow considerations—Jedi and Sith, light and dark. There's more to this galaxy that that.*"  
    "*Then what would you have me do?*"  
    "*Free yourself of the prison of your own making.*"
:   ―Qui-Gon Jinn offers Maul a new future[[77]](#cite_note-Ghosts-77)

 [![Qui-Gon Jinn, or at least a vision of him, appeared to Maul (Jinn as a Force spirit, pictured)](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/QuiGonJinn9BBY-OWKp6.png/revision/latest?cb=20250105064713) [![Qui-Gon Jinn, or at least a vision of him, appeared to Maul (Jinn as a Force spirit, pictured)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/QuiGonJinn9BBY-OWKp6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20250105064713)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/QuiGonJinn9BBY-OWKp6.png/revision/latest?cb=20250105064713) 

Qui-Gon Jinn, or at least a vision of him, appeared to Maul (Jinn as a Force spirit, pictured)

 

Maul made his way to the center of the temple, feeling a dark power drawing him forward with which he hoped to destroy his enemies. After wondering what kind of conflicts had been fought on the planet, Maul remained vigilant, unsure if he was being taunted or tested, but found himself shocked as he passed the final, simple door: behind sat a vision of Qui-Gon Jinn. Maul was certain the deceased Jedi Master wanted to engage in a final duel, but Jinn instead offered him a chance to walk away on a new path. Confirming he was not looking for Maul to become a Jedi by stating such an assumption was narrowminded, Jinn offered Maul a chance to free himself from the prison of his past, further asking what awaited him once Sidious and Kenobi were dead. Maul assumed that Jinn was taunting him to unleash his anger, but Jinn stated they both knew he was feeling pain from his losses, not rage. Jinn told Maul that his desire to hurt others would never heal his own pain, but Maul responded by attacking Jinn's specter.[[77]](#cite_note-Ghosts-77)

By the time he stopped, Maul realized that Jinn was gone and felt empty. Further, he could no longer feel the dark power that drew him to the castle in the first place. As such, Maul returned to his ship and considered firing upon the castle, but he decided temple was nothing to concern himself with. Focusing himself on his quest for vengeance, he charted a new course and continued his hunt for other dark secrets and Sith temples.[[77]](#cite_note-Ghosts-77)

#### Escape from Malachor

:   "*My apprentice is activating the temple, or more precisely, this battle station, which I shall use to exact my revenge on* all *my enemies!*"
:   ―Maul, to Ahsoka Tano[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

Maul's search for the Sith holocron eventually led him to the planet Malachor, where he would find the powerful weapon he sought in the Sith temple.[[26]](#cite_note-LaJE-26) Maul got frustrated with his inability to enter the temple.[[80]](#cite_note-HC_38-80) However, his ship became wrecked, leaving Maul a prisoner on the planet for years.[[26]](#cite_note-LaJE-26)

 [![Maul was trapped and alone on Malachor for years after returning to the planet to find a way to destroy the Sith.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/Hidden_Motive_SWDR.png/revision/latest?cb=20190618141510) [![Maul was trapped and alone on Malachor for years after returning to the planet to find a way to destroy the Sith.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/Hidden_Motive_SWDR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20190618141510)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/Hidden_Motive_SWDR.png/revision/latest?cb=20190618141510) 

Maul was trapped and alone on Malachor for years after returning to the planet to find a way to destroy the Sith.

 

Around the year [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY"), an Inquisitor known as the [Eighth Brother](/wiki/Eighth_Brother "Eighth Brother") tracked Maul to Malachor. It was also at this time that Maul [came in contact](/wiki/Mission_to_Malachor "Mission to Malachor") with Jedi apprentice [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger"), to whom he told that he had crashed his ship years prior, leaving him trapped without contact from the wider galaxy. Introducing himself as the "Old Master," whilst also posing as a feeble elderly man, Maul alleged he had been seeking the same Sith holocron that Bridger was searching for, also seeking to destroy the Sith. Maul offered to help Bridger claim the holocron, revealing it was located inside the temple. As Bridger agreed to work together to claim it, Maul began manipulating the young Jedi apprentice. During their time together, Maul told Bridger about his past, saying that the Sith had taken everything from him. As Bridger began to trust and relate to Maul even more, Maul also explained to Bridger the ways of the dark side, preying upon the boy's passionate and aggressive tendencies.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

The pair were able to retrieve the [Sith holocron](/wiki/Sith_holocron_(Malachor) "Sith holocron (Malachor)") after passing a series of physical challenges, with Maul guiding Bridger using the dark side. Advising him to use his feelings of loss and anger, Maul and Bridger discovered a key to reach the front of the temple, where they came across Jedi Knight [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") and Ahsoka Tano, who were members of [Phoenix Cell](/wiki/Phoenix_Cell "Phoenix Cell") from the nascent rebellion against the Empire. Seeing them in combat with Eighth Brother, [Fifth Brother](/wiki/Fifth_Brother "Fifth Brother"), and [Seventh Sister](/wiki/Seventh_Sister "Seventh Sister"), Maul led Bridger down to their position. While Tano and Jarrus were reluctant to trust Maul, with his help, the three of them forced the Inquisitors to retreat. Maul had learned of the Inquisitors' master, Darth Vader, and knew that they would inform him of the confrontation. This meant that Vader would soon be there, and Maul told the others that they would have to work together in order to defeat him.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

 [![Maul began to manipulate Ezra to further his own agenda and sow the seeds of darkness in him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Maul_and_Ezra.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160401173123) [![Maul began to manipulate Ezra to further his own agenda and sow the seeds of darkness in him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Maul_and_Ezra.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160401173123)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Maul_and_Ezra.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160401173123) 

Maul began to manipulate Ezra to further his own agenda and sow the seeds of darkness in him.

 

Still unwilling to trust Maul, they only cooperated with him at the behest of Bridger, who remained adamant that Maul was on their side. With Maul's guidance, the rebels scaled the temple in an attempt to reach the top, where Maul claimed they could find the knowledge they sought to defeat the Sith. Along the way, Maul and Bridger engaged the Seventh Sister, with Maul easily subduing her in a [Force choke](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke"). It was then that Maul implored Bridger to strike her down. Bridger hesitated, so Maul threw his lightsaber at her, killing her instantly. Maul scolded Bridger for his hesitation, warning him that it could cost him his life or the life of his friends in the future. Maul and Bridger continued on and met up with their other two companions, who were engaging the Fifth Brother and Eighth Brother in a lightsaber duel.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

It was then that Maul sensed the presence of Darth Vader, who was approaching Malachor. He, however, dismissed his feeling to Ezra when the young Jedi asked him what was wrong. Maul then engaged the Inquisitors while Bridger continued on alone. Maul, with Tano's assistance, slew the Fifth Brother, with Jarrus also managing to damage the Eighth Brother's lightsaber. As the Eighth Brother attempted to escape using his weapon, it malfunctioned, and the Inquisitor fell to his death below.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

 [![Sixteen years after the Siege of Mandalore, Maul and Tano fought again on the ancient Sith world of Malachor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/78/AhsokaTanoVsMaul-TOTA.png/revision/latest?cb=20161012054503) [![Sixteen years after the Siege of Mandalore, Maul and Tano fought again on the ancient Sith world of Malachor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/78/AhsokaTanoVsMaul-TOTA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161012054503)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/78/AhsokaTanoVsMaul-TOTA.png/revision/latest?cb=20161012054503) 

Sixteen years after the Siege of Mandalore, Maul and Tano fought again on the ancient Sith world of Malachor.

 

With all the Inquisitors dead and Ezra nearing the top, Maul then betrayed the Jedi, striking at Jarrus and blinding him. With Jarrus subdued, Maul engaged Tano and the two dueled briefly. It was then he revealed that the [holocron](/wiki/Holocron "Holocron") was intended to power an ancient [superweapon](/wiki/Malachor_superweapon "Malachor superweapon") and that Maul intended to make Bridger his apprentice. Tano left to get Bridger and confronted Darth Vader as Jarrus regained himself, with Tano claiming to the former Sith Lord he would have to face Jarrus to get to her. Underestimating Jarrus, Maul declared that he would finish off the Jedi quickly. However, using his other senses, amplified by the Force, Jarrus caught Maul's arm and tripped him, where the Nightbrother fell from the temple to the ground below.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

Maul survived the fall and eventually fled the planet using the [Eighth Brother](/wiki/Eighth_Brother "Eighth Brother")'s [TIE/ad v1](/wiki/Eighth_Brother%27s_TIE_fighter "Eighth Brother's TIE fighter"), following the destruction of the Sith temple on Malachor.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18) Realizing his plans were in ruins, Maul took a personal interest in Bridger.[[80]](#cite_note-HC_38-80) His influence had a profound effect on Bridger, who drifted closer to the dark side.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

#### Discovering Kenobi

:   "*He lives! He lives!*"
:   ―Maul on finding out that Obi-Wan Kenobi is still alive[[81]](#cite_note-THoF-81)

[Months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") later in [2 BBY](/wiki/2_BBY "2 BBY"), Maul resurfaced and continued to pursue the rebels. Managing to board a [*Sphyrna*-class Hammerhead corvette](/wiki/Sphyrna-class_Hammerhead_corvette "Sphyrna-class Hammerhead corvette"), Maul [interrogated](/wiki/Torture "Torture") one of the rebels on board, forcing him to reveal the location of the rebel [freighter](/wiki/VCX-100_light_freighter "VCX-100 light freighter"), and Ezra Bridger's home, the *[Ghost](/wiki/Ghost "Ghost")*. Shortly after, Bridger and Kanan Jarrus arrived at the transport and learned of the attack. Believing it to be the work of an Inquisitor, the pair contacted [Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Hera_Syndulla "Hera Syndulla"), the *Ghost*'s [pilot](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot"), and found out that Maul had taken her and the rest of the [crew](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres") hostage. In exchange for their friends' lives, Maul demanded the Jedi give him both the Sith holocron and the Jedi holocron, to which they agreed.[[81]](#cite_note-THoF-81)

While Jarrus and Bridger returned to the planet [Atollon](/wiki/Atollon "Atollon") to retrieve the Sith holocron, Maul softly demanded Syndulla give him a "tour" around the *Ghost*, prompting [Sabine Wren](/wiki/Sabine_Wren "Sabine Wren") to implore her not to, to which Maul replied she should trust him, for he did once rule her people. Surveying each living quarter, Maul identified Jarrus's as the dull and dour one, befitting of a Jedi. Instructing Syndulla to reveal the location of the Jedi holocron, the Twi'lek told Maul that she didn't know anything about Jarrus. Knowing this to be a lie, Maul probed her mind with the Force, and learned that it was Syndulla's idea to recruit Bridger, and that the boy once stole the holocron, which was being held in a compartment below Jarrus's bed.[[81]](#cite_note-THoF-81)

While Maul struggled to open the holocron, the *Ghost*'s crew took the opportunity to escape. Using their [restraints](/wiki/Stuncuffs "Stuncuffs") to destroy the reprogrammed [tour guide droids](/wiki/RIC-1200 "RIC-1200") guarding them, the rebels quietly moved down to the cargo hold, planning to [magnetize](/wiki/Magnet "Magnet") it in order to immobilize Maul's robotic legs. Discovering their absence, Maul went searching for the rebels and eventually made his way to the cargo hold. [Seconds](/wiki/Second "Second") later, the rebel crew's [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid"), [C1-10P](/wiki/C1-10P "C1-10P"), activated the magnets, causing Maul's legs to adhere to the vessel's ceiling. The rest of the rebels promptly rushed into the cargo hold and started firing at him; however, Maul deflected one of the bolts into the control interface, deactivating the magnets. Knocking the crew down with the Force, Maul threatened the rebels with their deaths once their usefulness was over.[[81]](#cite_note-THoF-81)

 [![Maul and Bridger combine the holocrons.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/The_Holocrons_of_Fate_Episode_Guide.png/revision/latest?cb=20161001154010) [![Maul and Bridger combine the holocrons.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/The_Holocrons_of_Fate_Episode_Guide.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161001154010)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/The_Holocrons_of_Fate_Episode_Guide.png/revision/latest?cb=20161001154010) 

Maul and Bridger combine the holocrons.

 

Having already informed the Jedi of their rendezvous point, the Mandalorian asteroid outpost, Maul landed the *Ghost* in one of its [hangars](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar") and kept the rebel prisoners under the watch of his reprogrammed droids. When the Jedi arrived, they met with Maul in the hangar, where the Dathomirian instructed Bridger to follow his droids to the command center, while Jarrus came with Maul. Looking to succeed where he failed on Malachor, Maul led the Jedi to an [airlock](/wiki/Airlock "Airlock") and pushed him in, proceeding to eject him into [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace"). Believing Jarrus to be dead, Maul went to meet Bridger, quietly instructing one of his droids to execute the rebel crew.[[81]](#cite_note-THoF-81)

Swapping holocrons, Maul and Bridger sat down on the floor and opened the devices, seeking to combine them and have their questions answered. After [combining](/wiki/Holocron_fusion "Holocron fusion") the holocrons, Bridger, who wanted to know the key to destroying the Sith, saw locations both familiar and unfamiliar, while Maul saw nothing. Shortly after, the *Ghost* crew, who had been freed by Jarrus after he made his way back into the hangar, arrived at the command center but were dazzled by the light coming from the holocrons. Bridger exclaimed that he saw "twin suns," and Jarrus implored his apprentice to look away, while Maul incited the Jedi to focus. Heeding his master's warning, Bridger closed his eyes, causing the energy from the holocrons to explode and giving Maul a chance to escape. As Maul proceeded back to his [ship](/wiki/Nightbrother_(Gauntlet_fighter) "Nightbrother (Gauntlet fighter)"), he realized what he had seen in the holocrons, repeating the phrase, "He lives."[[81]](#cite_note-THoF-81)

#### Return to Dathomir

:   "*Our futures converge on a planet with two suns. We can walk that path together as friends, as brothers.*"
:   ―Maul to Ezra Bridger on their shared vision[[82]](#cite_note-Visions_and_Voices-82)

Due to the ritual involving the two holocrons, Maul and Ezra became mentally linked, both gaining information of what they both desired. As a result, Maul found [Chopper Base](/wiki/Chopper_Base "Chopper Base") on the planet Atollon. Using his mastery of the dark side, Maul tormented Ezra by causing the young Jedi to see and hear visions of him. On one occasion, Ezra even attacked and almost killed a rebel trooper whom he mistook for Maul. Later, he approached Ezra and Kanan in the wilderness while they were talking to a mysterious [Force wielder](/wiki/Force_wielder "Force wielder") called [Bendu](/wiki/Bendu "Bendu"), who served as a bridge between the light and dark sides of the Force. Despite Bendu's warnings not to turn around, Kanan and Ezra did so and found Maul watching them from the top of a dune.[[82]](#cite_note-Visions_and_Voices-82)

After complimenting the two Jedi for their safe hiding place, Maul assured them that he had come in peace to talk with his "apprentice" Ezra. When Ezra demanded to know how Maul tracked him down, the dark sider replied that Ezra's abrupt severance of their connection to the holocrons caused them to see fragments of each other's visions and knowledge. Maul added that he needed Ezra to come with him in order to retrieve the remaining fragments of the vision from his mind. When Kanan refused to negotiate with Maul, the dark sider threatened to activate a [homing beacon](/wiki/Homing_beacon "Homing beacon") that would alert the Empire to their presence in the event of his death.[[82]](#cite_note-Visions_and_Voices-82)

Maul then offered to show Ezra how to destroy the Sith. With Kanan's reluctant approval, Ezra complied with Maul's ultimatum and departed with Maul on the *Nightbrother*. Maul took his unwilling apprentice to his homeworld of Dathomir. Unknown to them, Kanan and Sabine had placed a tracker on Ezra's [wrist comm](/wiki/Wrist_comm "Wrist comm") and followed them there. Maul took Ezra to the ruins of the [Nightsister lair](/wiki/Nightsister_lair "Nightsister lair") and explained that he was the last survivor of the Nightsisters. As Maul led Ezra into his cave-dwelling, he explained that the only way to retrieve the information was to merge their minds again in a ritual.[[82]](#cite_note-Visions_and_Voices-82)

 [![Maul spoke briefly about the Darksaber to Bridger, the legendary Mandalorian lightsaber that he had achieved in combat many years earlier.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Visions_and_Voices_thumb.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209220022) [![Maul spoke briefly about the Darksaber to Bridger, the legendary Mandalorian lightsaber that he had achieved in combat many years earlier.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Visions_and_Voices_thumb.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209220022)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Visions_and_Voices_thumb.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209220022) 

Maul spoke briefly about the Darksaber to Bridger, the legendary Mandalorian lightsaber that he had achieved in combat many years earlier.

 

Maul had the cave filled with relics from his past, including a damaged [portrait of Duchess Satine Kryze](/wiki/Painting_of_Duchess_Satine_Kryze "Painting of Duchess Satine Kryze") as well as the Darksaber, a Mandalorian symbol of power. For the ritual, Maul and Ezra drank glasses of [magick](/wiki/Magick "Magick") water which caused their eyes to turn green and shoot bright rays. As a result, Maul and Ezra discovered that his nemesis Obi-Wan Kenobi was hiding on a planet with twin suns and that Kenobi held the key to destroying the Sith. After completing the ritual, the two were confronted by Nightsister spirits that demanded that Maul and Ezra sacrifice their flesh and blood in return for the answers.[[82]](#cite_note-Visions_and_Voices-82)

At that point, Kanan and Sabine entered the cave and opened fire on the spirits. However, the spirits overwhelmed and possessed them. The possessed Kanan and Sabine attacked Maul and Ezra. Maul was forced to parry with the possessed Kanan while Ezra was forced to dodge the possessed Sabine's blasts. Following a struggle, Maul and Ezra reached the entrance of the cave. The Nightsister spirits were unable to leave, because the altar was the source of their power. Having accomplished his objective, Maul offered Ezra a place as his apprentice and claimed that their destiny was linked with the planet with the twin suns. However, Ezra refused to abandon his friends. Exasperated by the sympathy and compassion of the young man towards his friends, Maul told Ezra that he had disappointed him before leaving to find his old enemy, Obi-Wan Kenobi.[[82]](#cite_note-Visions_and_Voices-82)

#### Death on Tatooine

:   "*Tell me… Is it the Chosen One?*"  
    "*He is.*"  
    "*He… will… avenge us.*"
:   ―Maul's final words with Obi-Wan Kenobi, referencing Luke Skywalker[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

 [![In the Tatooine desert, Maul faced his enemy, Obi-Wan Kenobi, for the last time.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Twin_suns.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240318150936) [![In the Tatooine desert, Maul faced his enemy, Obi-Wan Kenobi, for the last time.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Twin_suns.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240318150936)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Twin_suns.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240318150936) 

In the Tatooine desert, Maul faced his enemy, Obi-Wan Kenobi, for the last time.

 

Maul eventually made his way to Tatooine, using knowledge from the two holocrons months earlier in search of his old nemesis Obi-Wan Kenobi. While searching for him in the desert wastes, Maul realized that he was lost. Exhausted from his search and contemplating the thought of dying in the desert, he collapsed into the sand and started screaming Kenobi's name in desperation. However, he found a renewed sense of determination and resumed his search for Kenobi. Knowing that he was unable to find his old enemy on his own, he planned to draw him out, using the matrix he had taken from the Sith holocron to reach out to his "apprentice," Ezra Bridger.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

Bridger, inspired by the vision sent by Maul, [traveled to Tatooine](/wiki/Mission_to_Tatooine_(Imperial_Era) "Mission to Tatooine (Imperial Era)") to prevent the former Sith Lord from killing Kenobi. The Jedi apprentice also hoped to recruit the old Jedi Master to join [the growing rebellion](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic"). Landing in a canyon at night, he discovered the fragment of the Sith holocron that Maul had planted as bait to lure him in. Deducing that it was a trap, he and his droid were suddenly ambushed by a band of [Tusken Raiders](/wiki/Tusken_Raider "Tusken Raider"), who attempted to kill Bridger. While the Tuskens failed to kill him, they did succeed in destroying the ship he arrived in. Shortly after Bridger was knocked unconscious by the explosion, Maul arrived and cut down all of the Tuskens before seemingly leaving Bridger alone.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

Seeking a way off-world, Bridger and Chopper, who had stowed away on Bridger's ship, debated whether to follow the natural ridgelines of the canyons in the hope of finding a nearby settlement or crossing the vast desert in front of them. Maul appeared in an apparition and convinced Ezra to travel into the desert. Ezra and Chopper traveled into the desert but the two collapsed due to a sandstorm. A short while later, Bridger and Chopper were discovered by Kenobi, who was riding a [dewback](/wiki/Dewback "Dewback"). Constructing a small campfire, Kenobi recharged Chopper with power from a portable light and tended to Bridger's wounds.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

After Ezra awoke, Kenobi told the boy that Maul had manipulated Ezra into leading the former Sith Lord to Kenobi. At that moment, Maul arrived to settle the score with his old archenemy. Having led Maul to Kenobi, Bridger insisted on fighting the former Sith himself, but Kenobi commanded Ezra to return to his friends. Ezra and Chopper left, with Maul bidding farewell to his "apprentice." Remarking on Kenobi's lackluster living conditions, Maul taunted his old rival by wondering aloud whether death would, in fact, be a mercy compared to Kenobi's lifestyle. Kenobi was unperturbed and responded by stating that because Maul defined himself by his empty desires to dominate, kill, and possess, he had nothing at all. Maul, stung by the verbal barb, ignited his lightsaber and struck the ground in front of Kenobi's small campfire, showering it with sand and snuffing it out. The former Sith Lord speculated on what could have brought Kenobi to Tatooine, knowing it was not simply hiding but deduced that he was there to protect something—or someone. He could see what was in Kenobi's thoughts: a boy.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

Stirred to action by Maul's threatening implications towards his charge, Kenobi activated his lightsaber and assumed the Soresu ready stance. Maul, in turn, activated the second blade of his weapon and the two enemies locked gazes. Kenobi switched his stance from Soresu to Ataru, and Maul recognized Kenobi's new stance as having belonged to Kenobi's old master Qui-Gon Jinn. He charged Kenobi, and the adversaries exchanged two rapid strikes before Maul brought the hilt of his blade up to strike Kenobi's face—the same attack which had allowed him to kill Jinn decades earlier. However, Kenobi had been prepared for Maul's strategy, and he brought his lightsaber down in an overhand strike as Maul initiated his attack. Kenobi's attack passed straight through the hilt of Maul's weapon,[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83) cleaving it in two and carving a lethal laceration into Maul's chest.[[44]](#cite_note-DBMaul-44)

 [![Despite his hatred, which persisted even during his many years of insanity in Lotho Minor, Maul died in Kenobi's arms, accepting his fate.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Maul_dies_but_for_real_this_time.png/revision/latest?cb=20170319062616) [![Despite his hatred, which persisted even during his many years of insanity in Lotho Minor, Maul died in Kenobi's arms, accepting his fate.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Maul_dies_but_for_real_this_time.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170319062616)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Maul_dies_but_for_real_this_time.png/revision/latest?cb=20170319062616) 

Despite his hatred, which persisted even during his many years of insanity in Lotho Minor, Maul died in Kenobi's arms, accepting his fate.

 

A shocked Maul looked down at his wound. Unlike last time, both ends of the lightsaber remained functional. He turned them off before dropping to one knee, but Kenobi caught him before he could fall to the ground and held him. Knowing that his death was inevitable this time, Maul then begged his sworn enemy to answer whether or not the boy that he was guarding was the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One"). Sensing Maul's pain and desperation for closure, Kenobi confirmed that the boy was indeed the one to fulfill the prophecy and destroy the Sith. With this knowledge, Maul seemed to come to terms with his death and, with his final breath, states that the boy will one day avenge what [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") had done to them both.

With that, after so many years of rage and anguish, Maul finally passed away peacefully,[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83) believing that his master's wrath would soon be over.[[84]](#cite_note-HC_51-84) As a final gesture of mercy, Kenobi closed his eyes and laid him to rest.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

### Legacy

#### Remainder of the Imperial Era

:   "*Tell me, child, do you know who I am? Do they whisper my name in the classrooms of your academy, down the winding halls of your space station, in the hollows and fields of your farming planet, or across the dunes of your desert home? If they do, what do they say of me? That I was once a great Sith Lord, apprenticed to the most powerful being in the galaxy? That I killed the legendary Jedi named Qui-Gon Jinn at the Battle of Naboo? Do they remember my glory? My distinctive black-and-red skin and horns? My unmatched skill with the double-bladed lightsaber? Or do they just remember how I died?*"
:   ―Maul considers his legacy[[45]](#cite_note-Dark_Vengeance-45)

Kenobi honored his old adversary by building him a funeral pyre, something he recalled shortly after becoming one with the Force.[[85]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-85) The Spectres' witness accounts and information on Maul were placed in the [Rebel Alliance Archives](/wiki/Rebel_Alliance_Archives "Rebel Alliance Archives").[[86]](#cite_note-RiseandFall-86) Maul's ship, the *Nightbrother*, was taken by Ezra and Chopper back to Chopper Base as a new vehicle for the Alliance. It was key in the [Battle of Atollon](/wiki/Battle_of_Atollon "Battle of Atollon"), in which Ezra and Sabine used it to transport members of [Clan Wren](/wiki/Clan_Wren "Clan Wren") to take down an [Imperial Interdictor](/wiki/Interdictor_(Interdictor-class) "Interdictor (Interdictor-class)") and allow the Rebels to escape [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Thrawn's](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo") blockade.[[87]](#cite_note-Zero_Hour-87)

Sidious considered Darth Maul to be a loss, whereas Count Dooku was labeled as both a [proton torpedo](/wiki/Proton_torpedo "Proton torpedo") and a mere placeholder.[[88]](#cite_note-EoG_1-88) While having a Force vision surrounding Luke Skywalker, Sidious appreciated that he was a simple boy not covered in demonic tattoos like those of Maul.[[89]](#cite_note-Disturbance-89)

Crimson Dawn continued to endure many years after Maul's death, but instead led by Qi'ra.[[90]](#cite_note-War_of_the_Bounty_Hunters_2-90) She hoped to do what Maul had wanted to do but couldn't and use Crimson Dawn to take down the Empire and the Sith who lead it.[[74]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_1-74) After Crimson Dawn revealed itself to the galaxy again between [3 ABY](/wiki/3_ABY "3 ABY") and [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY"),[[91]](#cite_note-Lando_quote_date-91) [Lando Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian") recalled the horrible actions of Crimson Dawn and its public leader, Dryden Vos, voicing speculation that Vos was overseen by an "even worse" individual.[[92]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_14-92)

Imperial [historians](/wiki/Historian "Historian") were aware of Maul's affiliation with Sheev Palpatine. Historical records noted that Maul was the owner of the heavily modified [Star Courier](/wiki/Star_Courier "Star Courier") the *Scimitar*. It was hypothesized that the *Scimitar* was customized by [Raith Sienar](/wiki/Raith_Sienar "Raith Sienar") for Palpatine, who then bestowed the ship to Maul.[[93]](#cite_note-TFOWM-93)

 [![Leia Organa, sensing the remnants of Maul](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/RemnantsOfMaul-ShatteredEmpire3.png/revision/latest?cb=20161002000637) [![Leia Organa, sensing the remnants of Maul](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/RemnantsOfMaul-ShatteredEmpire3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161002000637)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/RemnantsOfMaul-ShatteredEmpire3.png/revision/latest?cb=20161002000637) 

Leia Organa, sensing the remnants of Maul

 

Twenty-three years after the [end](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") of the Clone Wars, Palpatine's [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") was overthrown by the Alliance to Restore the Republic and the last Jedi Knight in the galaxy: Luke Skywalker,[[94]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-94) the son of Anakin Skywalker and Padmé Amidala.[[63]](#cite_note-Episode_III-63) Luke's [twin](/wiki/Twin "Twin") sister, [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), [traveled](/wiki/Battle_of_Theed "Battle of Theed") to Naboo shortly before [Operation: Cinder](/wiki/Operation:_Cinder "Operation: Cinder"), which forced her, the [queen](/wiki/Sosha_Soruna "Sosha Soruna"), and her escort [Shara Bey](/wiki/Shara_Bey "Shara Bey") to reopen the Theed Royal Palace hangar[[95]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_3-95)—where Maul dueled Qui-Gon Jinn and Obi-Wan Kenobi over three decades earlier[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)—in order to access starfighters. When she entered, Organa felt, through the Force, remnants of Maul's dark power, feeling physically cold because of it.[[95]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_3-95)

#### Post-Imperial era

:   "*According to these records, Maul was taken from his people on Dathomir at a young age and spent years learning from Palpatine but, following his defeat on Naboo, he was—although presumed dead for some time—discarded.*"
:   ―Beaumont Kin, *The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire*[[86]](#cite_note-RiseandFall-86)
