Following the fall of the Galactic Empire, Maul's manipulations over the Shadow Collective became public knowledge.[[96]](#cite_note-Species_From_A_to_Z-96) Maul was mentioned in the *[Galactic Explorer's Guide](/wiki/Galactic_Explorer%27s_Guide "Galactic Explorer's Guide")*, a survival guide written by Hondo Ohnaka and [DK-RA-43](/wiki/DK-RA-43 "DK-RA-43").[[24]](#cite_note-GEG-24)

By [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"), a bust of Maul could be found at [Dok-Ondar's Den of Antiquities](/wiki/Dok-Ondar%27s_Den_of_Antiquities "Dok-Ondar's Den of Antiquities"), one of the many shops in [Black Spire Outpost](/wiki/Black_Spire_Outpost "Black Spire Outpost") on [Batuu](/wiki/Batuu "Batuu").[[97]](#cite_note-D23_food_and_merch-97) Though it was believed that Palpatine had died in his confrontation with Luke Skywalker,[[94]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-94) he had in fact survived and continued his operations aided by the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal") [cult](/wiki/Sith_cult "Sith cult") on the planet [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol").[[98]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-98) In [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"),[[3]](#cite_note-Timelines-3) Sidious was permanently killed by the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") [Rey Skywalker](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") and the Sith Eternal was abolished through the efforts of the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance") at the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol").[[98]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-98) Following the battle, the Resistance launched the [Exegol Excavation Project](/wiki/Exegol_Excavation_Project "Exegol Excavation Project"), where files containing the biography of Darth Maul were discovered in the [Arcane Library](/wiki/Arcane_Library "Arcane Library"). In his [book](/wiki/Book "Book") *[The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire](/wiki/The_Rise_and_Fall_of_the_Galactic_Empire "The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire")* Resistance [historian](/wiki/Historian "Historian") [Beaumont Kin](/wiki/Beaumont_Kin "Beaumont Kin") included details about Maul's life, citing the uncovered Sith Eternal files as a source.[[86]](#cite_note-RiseandFall-86)

Maul was remembered long after the Clone Wars, and was mentioned by a [member](/wiki/Unidentified_second_Whill "Unidentified second Whill") of the [Whills](/wiki/Whills "Whills") as someone to be remembered in [galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history").[[99]](#cite_note-Whills-99)

## Personality and traits

:   "*If you define yourself by your power to take life, a desire to dominate, to possess, then you have nothing.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Maul[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

 [![Darth Maul once prided himself on his status as a Sith apprentice.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Darth_Maul_lightsaber_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20140421143551) [![Darth Maul once prided himself on his status as a Sith apprentice.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Darth_Maul_lightsaber_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20140421143551)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Darth_Maul_lightsaber_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20140421143551) 

Darth Maul once prided himself on his status as a Sith apprentice.

 

A former Sith Lord and a skilled warrior in his own right, Maul for most of his life came to embody the obsessive and frenzied aspects of Sith revenge. As a Sith apprentice, Maul sought revenge against the Jedi for their triumph over the Sith and wanted to return the Sith to power over the galaxy.[[1]](#cite_note-swe-Maul-1) After his exile and the restoration of his mind, Maul turned his thoughts of revenge towards the galaxy itself, declaring himself and his brother the true Sith Lords;[[12]](#cite_note-Eminence-12) and especially towards Obi-Wan Kenobi, after the Jedi defeated him and forced him into exile after their duel on Naboo. He felt the vacuum from losing power, having known about the Clone Wars and intending to be part of it, only to learn that the Sith plans moved on without him. Maul was, therefore, willing to go to great lengths to achieve his vengeance, including slaughtering civilians and thrusting Mandalore into civil war to gain power and draw Kenobi out into the open.[[9]](#cite_note-Revenge-9)[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) He knew the Jedi would not ignore a call for help.[[9]](#cite_note-Revenge-9)

Like all Sith,[[100]](#cite_note-DV:_SL-100) Maul's anger was his fuel. However, Maul still worked on his hatred. Maul felt there was so much to hate–from the fog of Dathomir to the way he had been cast aside as a child.[[21]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-21)

 [![Maul, shortly after his re-emergence at the time of the Clone Wars](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/DarkVengeance-TCWLightDark.png/revision/latest?cb=20240403101701) [![Maul, shortly after his re-emergence at the time of the Clone Wars](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/DarkVengeance-TCWLightDark.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240403101701)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/DarkVengeance-TCWLightDark.png/revision/latest?cb=20240403101701) 

Maul, shortly after his re-emergence at the time of the Clone Wars

 

During his exile, Maul's mind was shattered. He became obsessed with revenge,[[8]](#cite_note-Brothers-8) fueled and kept alive only by his hatred for Kenobi,[[9]](#cite_note-Revenge-9) despite losing his mind and many memories. His aggression and fear increased in his crazed condition, as Maul attacked Savage Opress when he first encountered his brother on Lotho Minor. When he was discovered by his brother, he could not speak coherently enough for Opress to understand him and would repeatedly recited lines from the [Code of the Sith](/wiki/Code_of_the_Sith "Code of the Sith").[[8]](#cite_note-Brothers-8) It required magic from Mother Talzin to restore his mind, bringing him clarity again while still preserving his desire to seek revenge against those who had wronged him.[[9]](#cite_note-Revenge-9) Maul's personality was still deeply affected by his isolation and defeat by Kenobi. After his restoration, he lost much of his taciturn bearing and was prone to outbursts of anger and frustration whenever Kenobi came to mind.[[12]](#cite_note-Eminence-12) However, he regained enough of his discipline to keep his brother Savage in line. He also retained his bloodthirsty nature.[[15]](#cite_note-Revival-15)

Maul's power made him crave dominance over the Sith and the galaxy, though he did not believe himself strong enough to take on his old mentor, Darth Sidious. It appeared that Sidious was the only being in the galaxy Maul ever feared, not only for his power but also his sadistic nature. Still, Maul had enough courage to take on his former master in open combat alone, as though he had nothing left to lose.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) And he would not break to either of Sidious and Count Dooku's torture sessions while incarcerated on Stygeon Prime.[[53]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_One-53)

 [![Maul allowed himself to be consumed by quests for vengeance.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Darth_Maul_1_Animation_textless.png/revision/latest?cb=20180119041627) [![Maul allowed himself to be consumed by quests for vengeance.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Darth_Maul_1_Animation_textless.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180119041627)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Darth_Maul_1_Animation_textless.png/revision/latest?cb=20180119041627) 

Maul allowed himself to be consumed by quests for vengeance.

 

Using fear to ensure his followers obeyed him, Maul sought riches and power as a crime lord.[[101]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunters_Stickers-101) Maul seemingly displayed a degree of honor[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57) despite considering it a weakness for the dark side[[12]](#cite_note-Eminence-12) as he freed the clone trooper Jesse when he no longer had a use for the soldier. Shortly later, however, he left his Mandalorian warriors to die.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57)

Despite his ruthless and vindictive nature, Maul was not completely heartless, as he displayed a genuine attachment for his brother, Savage Opress, and their mother, the Dathomir Witch Mother Talzin. He also knew how to forgive those he considered weak, such as the fleeing [Black Sun](/wiki/Black_Sun "Black Sun") members, who only downplayed him by not being rivals to him. Although Maul often ordered Savage around and defined their relationship in the Sith tradition of master and apprentice, much to Savage's chagrin, they did genuinely care about each other. This was shown when Maul jumped to Savage's defense when he was wounded by Kenobi, and backed down when he was threatened by Death Watch. Furthermore, after witnessing Savage being killed by Sidious, Maul was grief-stricken and briefly mourned him before flying into a rage and attempting to avenge him by beating Sidious.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) Maul was extremely loyal to his mother and reciprocated her loving and protective affection for him. Even when cornered by Sidious and his minions, he refused to leave her behind and was devastated by her death.[[55]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Four-55)

Even after many years, Maul still held an extremely bitter grudge against Sidious and all those who served him for taking everything he cared about from him. He also saw great potential in Ezra's abilities, desiring him as an apprentice, and even saving his life twice. However, he sought entirely to manipulate Bridger and use him to further his own obsessive agenda for power and revenge and attempted to kill Kanan Jarrus on two occasions in order to free Bridger of the Jedi's influence.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

 [![Maul saw aspects of himself in Ahsoka Tano, a fellow Force-Sensitive Outcast](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/ArtPrints-OneLastDuel.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126182655) [![Maul saw aspects of himself in Ahsoka Tano, a fellow Force-Sensitive Outcast](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/ArtPrints-OneLastDuel.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231126182655)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/ArtPrints-OneLastDuel.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126182655) 

Maul saw aspects of himself in Ahsoka Tano, a fellow Force-Sensitive Outcast

 

While still practicing their beliefs, Maul disassociated himself from the Sith, mainly due to the Order's association with Sidious. Cunning and deceptive, Maul was perfectly willing to feign weakness to accomplish his purposes, or even side with the Jedi if necessary. He was not above taunting such "allies," as evidenced by his calling Ahsoka "Lady Tano" and "a part-timer" in mockery of her departure from the Jedi Order[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18) as well as referring to Jarrus as "Master Jedi."[[81]](#cite_note-THoF-81) Maul also saw aspects of himself in Tano, noting how they had both departed their respective orders and saying they had both been used as "tools." He hoped to ally with her to defeat Sidious, but she rejected his offer when he revealed his visions of Anakin Skywalker's fall. All the same, he made yet another offer at the end of their duel[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57) and during Order 66.[[59]](#cite_note-Shattered-59)

Desiring hope, Maul kidnapped Bridger and Jarrus's rebel companions in a successful effort to force them to surrender the Sith holocron from Malachor and Kanan's [Jedi holocron](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus%27_holocron "Kanan Jarrus' holocron"). He wanted to merge the holocrons in order to create the clarity of vision needed to see his ultimate desire: Kenobi's death by his hand. Maul also hoped to take Ezra as his apprentice. Despite his promise to Bridger that he would not harm his friends, Maul secretly made an attempt on Jarrus's life and ordered his droids to execute the other Spectres in an attempt to claim Bridger as his apprentice. Despite Jarrus convincing Bridger to close his eyes and stop the vision, Maul nonetheless learned that his old enemy Obi-Wan Kenobi was still alive.[[81]](#cite_note-THoF-81)

 [![Maul, at the time of the Rebellion](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Maul_SWDL.png/revision/latest?cb=20211226235322) [![Maul, at the time of the Rebellion](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Maul_SWDL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20211226235322)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Maul_SWDL.png/revision/latest?cb=20211226235322) 

Maul, at the time of the Rebellion

 

Maul's still-burning desire for vengeance against Kenobi led him to use his mastery of the dark side to torment Bridger in an effort to gain his attention. While Maul was aware of the high price of Nightsister magic, his desire to learn Kenobi's location led him to risk the wrath of these spirits. Due to their revelations, Maul came to believe that his destiny was linked to finding and killing Kenobi on Tatooine. Maul regarded Bridger as an excellent candidate to be his apprentice. However, Bridger's attachment and loyalty to his friends angered Maul, who chastised his desired apprentice as a "disappointment" for refusing to break the chains of the past.[[82]](#cite_note-Visions_and_Voices-82)

Later, Maul's vendetta towards Kenobi led him to once again use his mastery of the Force to lure Bridger to Tatooine. Despite his hatred for Kenobi, before their battle he pondered if he should spare him after seeing he was reduced to hiding on the desert planet. Maul reconciled with his adversary in his last moments. Maul passed away with the belief that Kenobi was protecting the Chosen One who would restore balance to the Force and avenge them by destroying the Sith.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

This concludes that Maul was not entirely the monster that most saw him as, but truly a tragic character who had lost everything he cared about due to Darth Sidious' actions (much like his successor Darth Vader), but showed that he could not let go of his hate until his final moments.

## Powers and abilities

### Lightsaber abilities

:   "*You have been well trained, my young apprentice. They will be no match for you.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious orders Darth Maul to move against the Jedi during the war on Naboo[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

 [![Darth Maul was a fierce warrior, able to easily engage two Jedi in battle.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/AoR-DarthMaul-art.png/revision/latest?cb=20190626132639) [![Darth Maul was a fierce warrior, able to easily engage two Jedi in battle.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/AoR-DarthMaul-art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20190626132639)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/AoR-DarthMaul-art.png/revision/latest?cb=20190626132639) 

Darth Maul was a fierce warrior, able to easily engage two Jedi in battle.

 

As the apprentice of Darth Sidious, Maul was trained to be a living weapon of the Sith, one intended to help Sidious bring about the destruction of the Jedi and take over the galaxy. Under Sidious' tutelage, Maul became one of the deadliest, most efficiently trained Sith in the Order's history.[[102]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-102) He became an acrobatic and highly trained Sith warrior, one who could relentlessly pursue his enemies while utilizing his double-bladed lightsaber.[[1]](#cite_note-swe-Maul-1) Indeed, Maul had been trained in several forms of lightsaber combat. He put these skills to the test for the first time in his duel against the Jedi apprentice Eldra Kaitis; although the young Twi'lek managed to hold her own against the Sith for a time, Maul came out of the encounter victorious.[[36]](#cite_note-Darth_Maul_5-36) Later, during his duel on Naboo against Jinn and Kenobi, he demonstrated the ability to fight both the Jedi Master and his prodigious apprentice simultaneously on equal grounds as well as overpower Kenobi after he killed Jinn.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

Although Kenobi defeated Maul, this was in part due to Maul's own hubris and neglect for the fallen Jinn's lightsaber.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) He later outmatched Kenobi in a number of encounters after emerging from exile, including the fight over Raydonia,[[9]](#cite_note-Revenge-9) though their duel on Florrum ended in stalemate.[[15]](#cite_note-Revival-15) Maul was also extremely skilled in unarmed combat, which he often integrated into his fighting style.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52)[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18) This was most notable when he defeated an armed Pre Vizsla with little to no assistance from the Force.[[50]](#cite_note-SoR-50)

 [![Maul revealing his double-bladed lightsaber on Naboo](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/DarthMaul-SWD.png/revision/latest?cb=20190427215256) [![Maul revealing his double-bladed lightsaber on Naboo](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/DarthMaul-SWD.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20190427215256)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/DarthMaul-SWD.png/revision/latest?cb=20190427215256) 

Maul revealing his double-bladed lightsaber on Naboo

 

Maul also displayed considerable skill in [Jar'Kai](/wiki/Jar%27Kai "Jar'Kai"), holding his own against Jinn and Kenobi simultaneously on Naboo before splitting them up.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) He even put up a reasonable fight against Darth Sidious on Mandalore when they dueled with dual blades, going as far as landing a kick on the Dark Lord.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) After the Clone Wars, Maul demonstrated the ability to wield an additional weapon alongside his double-bladed lightsaber, on one occasion using a walking stick as a club in conjunction with his connected blades.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

Maul could destroy numerous enemies, including Banking Clan droid guards, pirates,[[15]](#cite_note-Revival-15) Hutt Clan forces,[[12]](#cite_note-Eminence-12) hordes of Separatist battle droids, clone troopers,[[62]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-62) and four of General Grievous' MagnaGuards.[[53]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_One-53) He also held his own against Mace Windu and Aayla Secura on a Mandalorian supply outpost, the elder Jedi being a longtime famed member of the High Council; this was a fight that Maul deemed "fair."[[11]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Three-11) He successfully overpowered the infamous Jedi hunter General Grievous,[[53]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_One-53) though he fought to a stalemate[[103]](#cite_note-AEYNTKEU-103) with the cyborg in their first, as he was more than equal for him,[[53]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_One-53) and second duel; he overwhelmed him in their second encounter, taking advantage of the cyborg's distraction.[[55]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Four-55)

 [![Maul's cane-disguised lightsaber](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/Maul_lightsaber.png/revision/latest?cb=20160428060959) [![Maul's cane-disguised lightsaber](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/Maul_lightsaber.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/148?cb=20160428060959)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/Maul_lightsaber.png/revision/latest?cb=20160428060959) 

Maul's cane-disguised lightsaber

 

Over a decade later, Maul's fighting prowess was still as sharp as ever. While on Malachor, he aided Ahsoka Tano and Kanan Jarrus against three members of the Inquisitorius, defeating them easily. He also battled Tano and Jarrus, in turn, but lost the high ground to Jarrus whom he blinded with his lightsaber.[[104]](#cite_note-Twilight_Episode_Gallery-104)

 [![Maul's swordsmanship was ultimately not a match for his former master.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/SidiousVsMaul-TL.png/revision/latest?cb=20131025203833) [![Maul's swordsmanship was ultimately not a match for his former master.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/SidiousVsMaul-TL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20131025203833)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/SidiousVsMaul-TL.png/revision/latest?cb=20131025203833) 

Maul's swordsmanship was ultimately not a match for his former master.

 

Despite Maul's dueling skills, Darth Sidious defeated both him and his brother Savage Opress. Though he pressed Sidious on his back foot, he was disarmed before being manhandled by the elder Sith Lord's Force powers.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) In his final duel, Maul was fatally wounded within seconds of challenging his old rival, Obi-Wan Kenobi.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

Unlike the Inquisitorius, whose [lightsabers](/wiki/Double-bladed_spinning_lightsaber "Double-bladed spinning lightsaber") could rotate,[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18) and General Grievous, whose split arms were able to spin with a weapon in each hand,[[105]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-105) Maul had the ability to twirl a double-bladed lightsaber with the use of only one hand.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)[[36]](#cite_note-Darth_Maul_5-36)

Maul was also very skilled at deflecting [blaster](/wiki/Blaster "Blaster") bolts with his lightsaber. He deflected the combined shots of Hera Syndulla, Sabine Wren and Zeb Orrelios, even when he was in a disadvantageous position.[[81]](#cite_note-THoF-81)

### Force powers

:   "*My hatred kept my spirit intact even though my body was not. Yet, I was lost and became a rabid animal, and such is how you found me, brother: discarded, forgotten. I have missed so much...*"
:   ―Maul, to Savage Opress[[9]](#cite_note-Revenge-9)

 [![Maul pulls a clone trooper towards him to sever the soldier's arm in a closing door](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/ThisIsGonnaHurt-Shattered.png/revision/latest?cb=20200803050221) [![Maul pulls a clone trooper towards him to sever the soldier's arm in a closing door](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/ThisIsGonnaHurt-Shattered.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20200803050221)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/ThisIsGonnaHurt-Shattered.png/revision/latest?cb=20200803050221) 

Maul pulls a clone trooper towards him to sever the soldier's arm in a closing door

 

In addition to his expertise with a lightsaber, Maul proved to be very strong with the Force, strong enough to survive being cut in half.[[8]](#cite_note-Brothers-8) This, in Maul's belief, had been due to his hatred of Kenobi and Sidious' training.[[9]](#cite_note-Revenge-9) He was able to draw power from the [Dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") to make himself resistant to poisons.[[106]](#cite_note-SWA_(2020)_3-106)

Maul was able to use [Force deflection](/wiki/Force_deflection "Force deflection") to redirect blaster bolts against his enemies without using a lightsaber, and could guide his lightsaber through telekinesis after throwing it before having it return to his hand.[[107]](#cite_note-Darth_Maul:_BWR_3-107)
During a skirmish on Florrum, Maul used a [Force push](/wiki/Force_push "Force push") powerful enough to blast Obi-Wan Kenobi over a long distance and cause the tunnel they were in to collapse. He was later able to telekinetically drag an [*Eta*-class shuttle](/wiki/Eta-class_shuttle "Eta-class shuttle") from a plateau immediately after sustaining heavy injuries resulting in the loss of one of his cybernetic legs.[[15]](#cite_note-Revival-15) During his time on Mandalore, he was able to Force choke Satine Kryze to the point where he could hold her in midair without a hand gesture, a testament to his continued development.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) During the Battle of Zanbar, he unleashed a massive Force Wave that swept away many battle droids.[[53]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_One-53)

 [![Maul, former Sith Lord and leader of Crimson Dawn](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/Maul_SASWS_Forbes_Promo_full.png/revision/latest?cb=20180908015153) [![Maul, former Sith Lord and leader of Crimson Dawn](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/Maul_SASWS_Forbes_Promo_full.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/199?cb=20180908015153)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/Maul_SASWS_Forbes_Promo_full.png/revision/latest?cb=20180908015153) 

Maul, former Sith Lord and leader of Crimson Dawn

 

As the dark side of the Force became stronger within the galaxy during the time of Order 66, Maul's level of sheer strength grew as well for a brief time. He demonstrated the ability to telekinetically affect pure energy in the form of blaster bolts, effortlessly causing the rounds fired at him by Bo-Katan to bend and veer out of his path and into the nearby walls just by waving his hand. Shortly after his capture during the [Siege of Mandalore](/wiki/Siege_of_Mandalore "Siege of Mandalore"), Maul was released by Ahsoka Tano when Order 66 was issued and the clones turned against her. After being released, Maul murdered several clones using only his telekinetic abilities, tearing panels off the walls to defend himself from the shots and crush and decapitate the clones. The rampage ultimately culminated in Maul disabling the [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer"), which had been ferrying the renegade Sith, solely through his mastery of the Force. He used the Force to crush the massive hyperdrive generators of the Venator [Tribunal](/wiki/Tribunal "Tribunal"), resulting in its complete destruction.[[62]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-62) Over a decade later, Maul told Ezra Bridger that his advanced age had diminished his abilities. However, this was later revealed to have been a deception meant to gain the boy's trust. Indeed, Maul had been able to Force Grip the Seventh Sister against her active resistance while simultaneously killing her with a Saber Throw.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18)

 [![Maul was a well-trained assassin proficient in lightsaber combat who also possessed great power in the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/Darth_Maul_1_Albuquerque.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161124145410) [![Maul was a well-trained assassin proficient in lightsaber combat who also possessed great power in the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/Darth_Maul_1_Albuquerque.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/266?cb=20161124145410)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/Darth_Maul_1_Albuquerque.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161124145410) 

Maul was a well-trained assassin proficient in lightsaber combat who also possessed great power in the Force.

 

Maul was also skilled in [telepathy](/wiki/Telepathy "Telepathy"), specifically the mind probe technique, as shown when he used the power on Hera to find the location of Kanan Jarrus's Jedi holocron and his true identity;[[81]](#cite_note-THoF-81) he had even succeeded in using the technique on Obi-Wan Kenobi prior to their final duel, discovering the existence of Luke Skywalker.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83) It is not improbable that he employed it on Ahsoka Tano, learning much about her past,[[108]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-108) and it was likely that he probed the minds of the Inquisitors to decipher their intentions and the name of their master.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18) Maul was also familiar with the [magick](/wiki/Magick "Magick") practices of the [Nightsisters](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters"), including a scrying spell which involved two people sharing a [potion](/wiki/Merging_potion "Merging potion") of [magical ichor](/wiki/Magical_ichor "Magical ichor").[[82]](#cite_note-Visions_and_Voices-82) He was able to manipulate the [Force-bond](/wiki/Force-bond "Force-bond") he gained with Ezra Bridger as a result of holocron fusion to cause the young Jedi to hallucinate. He also used the fragment of a Sith holocron to activate Kanan's Jedi holocron and the Malachor Sith holocron as part of a plot to trick Ezra into luring Kenobi out of hiding.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

Even so, by the time of the Clone Wars, Maul's Force powers were still outclassed by those of Sidious, as the Dark Lord telekinetically pinned both him and Opress to a wall with no visible effort.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) But, as Maul had grown more powerful,[[15]](#cite_note-Revival-15) Sidious nonetheless considered him to be a rival.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) Darth Tyranus evidently thought rather highly of Maul, as he at one time referred to his predecessor as a great Sith Lord.[[109]](#cite_note-Monster-109) Obi-Wan Kenobi, prior to his and Maul's final duel, said that his old enemy had the power to "alter the course of many things," which would indicate Maul's vast knowledge of the dark side.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

### Other abilities

:   "*Far above, far below, we don't know where we'll fall. Far above, far below, what once was great is rendered small.*"
:   ―Mantra taught to Maul to help him focus his rage[[29]](#cite_note-maul-marvel-mini-2-29)

 [![Maul once claimed that a battle against two powerful Jedi was "a fair fight](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/MaulSecuraWindu-SoD3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190115214704) [![Maul once claimed that a battle against two powerful Jedi was "a fair fight](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/MaulSecuraWindu-SoD3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20190115214704)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/MaulSecuraWindu-SoD3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190115214704) 

Maul once claimed that a battle against two powerful Jedi was "a fair fight."

 

Maul was a capable manipulator and a skilled military and political strategist as demonstrated by, amongst other achievements, forming the Shadow Collective in a very short amount of time and use it to conquer Mandalore.[[12]](#cite_note-Eminence-12) He had enough cunning to trick and capture both General Grievous and Darth Tyranus in a single stroke.[[54]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Two-54) Earlier, Maul must have surveyed the Theed power generator on Naboo before his Jedi adversaries arrived, thus setting a trap for them.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

After being rescued by Death Watch, Maul said that he had become "indifferent to pain," suggesting a high pain threshold.[[53]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_One-53) Maul was experienced in surveillance, tracking, and espionage, acting primarily as a covert operative during his apprenticeship.[[33]](#cite_note-maul-marvel-mini-1-33) Maul showed exceptional agility and was skilled in [hand-to-hand combat](/wiki/Unarmed_combat "Unarmed combat").[[61]](#cite_note-TCW_Character_Encyclopedia-61)

## Equipment

### Overview

:   "*I like your new legs. They make you look taller.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Maul[[9]](#cite_note-Revenge-9)

 [![Under Sidious' tutelage, Darth Maul had a set of equipment under his employ which he kept in his ship, the Scimitar.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Sith_Infiltrator_SWCT.png/revision/latest?cb=20251112041636) [![Under Sidious' tutelage, Darth Maul had a set of equipment under his employ which he kept in his ship, the Scimitar.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Sith_Infiltrator_SWCT.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20251112041636)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Sith_Infiltrator_SWCT.png/revision/latest?cb=20251112041636) 

Under Sidious' tutelage, Darth Maul had a set of equipment under his employ which he kept in his ship, the *Scimitar*.

 

During the Naboo Crisis Maul wore Sith [clothing](/wiki/Clothing "Clothing") that allowed freedom of movement, including loose-fitting pants for high-kicks. Under a black cloak he wore an undertunic, heavy-action [boots](/wiki/Boot "Boot"), and protective [gloves](/wiki/Glove "Glove").[[110]](#cite_note-VE-110) At some point, the [R3-series astromech droid](/wiki/R3-series_astromech_droid "R3-series astromech droid") [R3-B0017](/wiki/R3-B0017 "R3-B0017") was programmed to serve Maul and scavenge Dathomir.[[111]](#cite_note-R3-B0017-111)

Maul's *Scimitar* was believed to be the deadliest Sith vessel ever built by the time of its creation. It was armed with six [laser cannons](/wiki/Laser_cannon "Laser cannon"), [spy](/wiki/Spy "Spy") and surveillance gear, [interrogator droids](/wiki/Interrogation_droid "Interrogation droid"), and a [cloaking device](/wiki/Cloaking_device "Cloaking device"). The ship carried Maul's [Razalon](/wiki/Razalon "Razalon") [FC-20 speeder bike](/wiki/FC-20_speeder_bike "FC-20 speeder bike"), the *Bloodfin*.[[112]](#cite_note-BMF_44-112)

### Lightsabers

 [![Maul wields his first lightsaber](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Star_Wars_Darth_Maul_1_textless.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180429204933) [![Maul wields his first lightsaber](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Star_Wars_Darth_Maul_1_textless.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180429204933)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Star_Wars_Darth_Maul_1_textless.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180429204933) 

Maul wields his first lightsaber

 

Maul's first lightsaber was a double-bladed lightsaber he wielded in the Invasion of Naboo[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) and the Clone Wars.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) It was cut in half by Obi-Wan Kenobi during their duel on Naboo,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) and Maul continued to use the remaining half in several battles until he temporarily lost it in his duel with his former master on Mandalore.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) He recovered the half after being freed from prison, and reformed it into a double-bladed hilt but lost it for good after a duel with Ahsoka Tano.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-57)

Maul's second lightsaber was the Darksaber, which he wielded against his former master on Mandalore[[52]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-52) and later against Grievous, although he was forced to retreat.[[53]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_One-53) Maul continued to use the Darksaber in several subsequent battles, such as the [battle of Ord Mantell](/wiki/Battle_on_Ord_Mantell "Battle on Ord Mantell"),[[54]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Two-54) the assault on Vizsla Keep 09,[[11]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Three-11) and the Second Battle of Dathomir.[[55]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir,_Part_Four-55)

 [![Maul's new lightsaber was design as a cane and appeared as if it was originally a double-bladed spinning lightsaber](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/MaulsInquisitorLightsaber-SWTLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20210107221109) [![Maul's new lightsaber was design as a cane and appeared as if it was originally a double-bladed spinning lightsaber](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/MaulsInquisitorLightsaber-SWTLC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210107221109)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/MaulsInquisitorLightsaber-SWTLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20210107221109) 

Maul's new lightsaber was design as a cane and appeared as if it was originally a double-bladed spinning lightsaber

 

Maul's third and final lightsaber was a new double-bladed lightsaber which was also a [cane lightsaber](/wiki/Sabercane "Sabercane"). The lightsaber produced two crimson-[red](/wiki/Color "Color") blades, and the upper grip-guard resembled that of the Inquisitors' lightsabers, albeit broken and bent outward.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18) Indeed, the lightsaber appeared as if it had been built out of pieces retrieved from an Inquisitor's blade.[[113]](#cite_note-Mini_Book_of_Lightsabers2-113) He would hide the hilt by attaching a piece of [wood](/wiki/Wood "Wood") to it, and pretending it was a walking stick, all the while masquerading as a feeble old man.[[18]](#cite_note-Twilight-18) Maul later used it on his hunt for his old nemesis Obi-Wan Kenobi. It was in this final duel that Maul was defeated, the lightsaber was bisected in a similar manner to his first when Kenobi sliced it in two. However, unlike last time, both halves of the lightsaber remained functional, only deactivating when Maul lost grip of them as he succumbed to his wounds.[[83]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-83)

## Behind the scenes

### Appearances

Darth Maul first appeared in [*Star Wars*: Episode I *The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), where he was played by actor and martial artist [Ray Park](/wiki/Ray_Park "Ray Park"). The character was a presence throughout the film, but only spoke three lines in total—all of which were voiced by actor [Peter Serafinowicz](/wiki/Peter_Serafinowicz "Peter Serafinowicz").[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) For the character's appearances in the animated television series *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* and *[Star Wars Rebels](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels "Star Wars Rebels")*, he was voiced by actor [Sam Witwer](/wiki/Sam_Witwer "Sam Witwer") (who also voiced [Starkiller](/wiki/Galen_Marek "Galen Marek") in the [Force Unleashed](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Force_Unleashed "Star Wars: The Force Unleashed") games).[[8]](#cite_note-Brothers-8) Park provided motion capture reference for the [seventh season](/wiki/The_Clone_Wars:_Season_Seven "The Clone Wars: Season Seven") of the former.[[114]](#cite_note-SW-SWCC_2019:_9_Things_We_Learned_from_the_''Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars''_Panel-114) For Maul's cameo in the [2018](/wiki/2018 "2018") [*Star Wars* Anthology](/wiki/Star_Wars_Anthology_Series "Star Wars Anthology Series") film *[Solo: A Star Wars Story](/wiki/Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story "Solo: A Star Wars Story")*, Park reprised the role and Witwer provided the character's voice.[[14]](#cite_note-Solo-14) The *Solo* script only specified a "Boss" character; director [Ron Howard](/wiki/Ron_Howard "Ron Howard") chose Maul from a list of possible candidates.[[115]](#cite_note-115)

### Development

:   "*George Lucas had described Darth Maul as a figure from your worst nightmare. So... I drew George my worst nightmare.*"
:   ―Iain McCaig, describing how he designed Darth Maul[[116]](#cite_note-DesigningSithLord-116)

 [![An early concept design for Darth Maul, straight out of Iain McCaig's nightmares](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bd/SithWitch.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100220052841) [![An early concept design for Darth Maul, straight out of Iain McCaig's nightmares](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bd/SithWitch.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/221?cb=20100220052841)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bd/SithWitch.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100220052841) 

An early concept design for Darth Maul, straight out of Iain McCaig's nightmares

 

For *The Phantom Menace*, the character was designed by concept designer [Iain McCaig](/wiki/Iain_McCaig "Iain McCaig"), who felt that designing a new *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* villain was daunting. He recalled [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") describing Maul as "a figure from your worst nightmare," so McCaig thought about his worst nightmares and used those to design an initial look for the character. McCaig described his worst nightmare as a lifeless face pressed against a window in a thunderstorm, a dead yet alive figure who stares at him through the rain. McCaig used that as the first design, adding metal teeth and blood-red ribbons falling on it rather than rain. Lucas apparently felt it was too intense, saying "Okay. Now draw me your second worst nightmare..."[[116]](#cite_note-DesigningSithLord-116)

McCaig spent much of the three-year pre-production time drawing masks, attempting to design something similar to [Ralph McQuarrie](/wiki/Ralph_McQuarrie "Ralph McQuarrie")'s original design for Darth Vader from [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"). Eventually, however, he felt he was on the wrong track. He ended up finding his stride when he drew members of the Episode I Art Department as Sith Lords, using their personalities and faces to design characters. At one point, McCaig used a circuit board as a face, a design that intrigued Lucas. Lucas also liked a concept based on production photographer Greg Gawlowski.[[116]](#cite_note-DesigningSithLord-116)

 [![Maul's final concept art by Iain McCaig](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/AoR-DarthMaul-D.png/revision/latest?cb=20190626132752) [![Maul's final concept art by Iain McCaig](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/AoR-DarthMaul-D.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/221?cb=20190626132752)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/AoR-DarthMaul-D.png/revision/latest?cb=20190626132752) 

Maul's final concept art by Iain McCaig

 

Darth Maul's design went through a number of other variations until McCaig created a series of Rorschach designs by creating splattered ink patterns, which led to the tattooed look of Darth Maul. McCaig wanted to soften the look of the character, at one point adding feathers the top of Darth Maul's head. McCaig saw these feathers are being part of the Sith Lord's personality; "every morning I imagined Darth Maul would get up and bind his head with this piano wire, and that the feathers had to end up at the right points—it was just a part of the focusing of the Sith." These feathers were interpreted as horns, however, which became part of the final design.[[116]](#cite_note-DesigningSithLord-116)

With the face of the character completed, McCaig also designed Maul's costume. Originally, Maul wore a large muscle suit, "making him larger than life," with Batman-like spikes on his neck. That costume made it through most of the storyboarding process until McCaig changed the costume and made it smaller after Lucas talked about an acrobatic lightsaber duel. The costume was therefore made smaller, resulting in the Sith robes Maul wore in *The Phantom Menace*.[[116]](#cite_note-DesigningSithLord-116) In the [February](/wiki/February "February") 1999 issue of *[Vanity Fair](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vanity_Fair "wikipedia:Vanity Fair")* promoting the film, Maul was identified as a menacing "pre-Vader dark side Jedi" despite Lucas making reference to Sidious as a Sith in the same interview. Also described as a mysterious figure, Maul was pictured in a lightsaber battle against Kenobi in a promotional image of Tatooine included in the issue.[[117]](#cite_note-The_Force_is_Back-117)

### Return to life

 [![The Infinities illustration that inspired Maul's look for The Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/DarthMaul-Visionaries.png/revision/latest?cb=20221116005242) [![The Infinities illustration that inspired Maul's look for The Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/DarthMaul-Visionaries.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20221116005242)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/DarthMaul-Visionaries.png/revision/latest?cb=20221116005242) 

The *Infinities* illustration that inspired Maul's look for *The Clone Wars*.

 

For his return in *The Clone Wars*, Witwer knew that Maul was a popular character and felt a responsibility to get it right and respect the character's iconic status. He described Maul as broken and attempted to convey a shattered mind through his acting. One way of doing so was to quote the [Code of the Sith](/wiki/Code_of_the_Sith "Code of the Sith") from the [Expanded Universe](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends"), part of which made it into the episode.[[118]](#cite_note-SamWitwerYouTube-118) The character's design on the show was very similar to his look in *The Phantom Menace*, and the animators used the designing of the character as an opportunity to improve animation on the series. Because the character's appearances required him to show emotion such as anger and hatred using only facial expressions, the animators spent time improving the modeling process to achieve better expressions. Because Maul had been cut in half in *The Phantom Menace*, he required a new set of cybernetic legs for *The Clone Wars*. The cyborg form of Darth Maul had previously been created by [Industrial Light & Magic](/wiki/Industrial_Light_%26_Magic "Industrial Light & Magic") concept artist [Aaron McBride](/wiki/Aaron_McBride "Aaron McBride") for the *[Infinities](/wiki/Infinities "Infinities")* graphic novel *[Star Wars: Visionaries](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Visionaries "Star Wars: Visionaries")*.[[119]](#cite_note-Explore:_Revenge-119)

Lucas originally planned to use the aged Maul as a villain in the [sequel trilogy](/wiki/Sequel_trilogy "Sequel trilogy"), taking on the Legends character [Darth Talon](/wiki/Darth_Talon "Darth Talon") as an apprentice, and becoming "the godfather of crime in the universe."[[120]](#cite_note-SW_Archives-120) Although the Zabrak never appeared in the sequel films, the idea of a crime lord Maul was later brought to live action in 2018's *Solo: A Star Wars Story*.[[14]](#cite_note-Solo-14) While developing the [second season](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels_Season_Two "Star Wars Rebels Season Two") of *Rebels*, it was initially intended for Maul to die at the hands of Darth Vader in the season finale "[Twilight of the Apprentice](/wiki/Twilight_of_the_Apprentice "Twilight of the Apprentice")," but it became unwieldy as there were too many storylines and not enough emotional material between Maul and Vader.[[121]](#cite_note-Vader_Maul-121)

To prevent leaks about Maul's appearance as the true leader of Crimson Dawn in *Solo: A Star Wars Story*, he went unnamed in the script, even causing some of the filmmakers to think the decision of who was Crimson Dawn's leader was still undecided.[[122]](#cite_note-Jon's_Tweet_1-122) Prior to Maul's selection, the first draft of the film's script had Dryden Vos as Crimson Dawn's second-in-command with a [Hume Cronyn](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hume_Cronyn "wikipedia:Hume Cronyn")–esque genial but ruthless character known as [The Kazier](/wiki/The_Kazier "The Kazier").[[123]](#cite_note-Jon's_Tweet_2-123) While Sam Witwer voiced Maul in the finished film, Maul's original voice actor Peter Serafinowicz initially recorded Maul's lines for the film, but his performance was ultimately cut in favor of Witwer's.[[124]](#cite_note-Serafinowicz_Cut_from_Solo-124)

### In the fandom

Since his first appearance in the trailer for *The Phantom Menace*, Maul has been a hit amongst the *Star Wars* fandom.[[125]](#cite_note-Faith_Fervor-125) On May 4, 2015, a costume of Darth Maul was added to [*The Sims 4*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Sims_4 "wikipedia:The Sims 4") for playable Sims to wear in-game. The costume is purely cosmetic and offers no gameplay changes.[[126]](#cite_note-Sims_4-126)

### Contradictions

The description blurb for the *[Witches of Dathomir Squad Pack](/wiki/Witches_of_Dathomir_Squad_Pack "Witches of Dathomir Squad Pack")* stated that Savage Opress was the oldest of Mother Talzin's sons, which would make Maul his younger sibling.[[127]](#cite_note-Witches_Squad_Pack-127) However, Opress's own Databank Download page for the set stated Maul was older than him.[[128]](#cite_note-Savage_preview-128) As such, this article does not assume which of the two was born first.

[*Star Wars The Dark Side Pocket Expert*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Dark_Side_Pocket_Expert "Star Wars: The Dark Side Pocket Expert") mistakenly lists Maul's height as 1.83 [meters](/wiki/Meter "Meter").[[129]](#cite_note-Dark_Side_Pocket_Expert-129)

A [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016") databank card posted on the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [Facebook](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Facebook "wikipedia:Facebook") account incorrectly spelled Maul's species as Dathomirian 'Zabrack.'[[130]](#cite_note-Maul_FB_photo_2016-130)

[↑](#cite_ref-Mon_Cala_Date_68-0) According to *[Ultimate Star Wars, New Edition](/wiki/Ultimate_Star_Wars,_New_Edition "Ultimate Star Wars, New Edition")*, the occupation of Mon Cala took place a year into the [Emperor's](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") rule. Since *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates the beginning of Imperial rule to [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), the occupation of Mon Cala took place in [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"). 69. [↑](#cite_ref-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_17_69-0) [*Darth Vader* (2017) 17](/wiki/Darth_Vader_(2017)_17 "Darth Vader (2017) 17") 70. [↑](#cite_ref-Star_Wars_15_date_70-0) [*Star Wars* (2015) 7](/wiki/Star_Wars_(2015)_7 "Star Wars (2015) 7") takes place a [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before [*Star Wars* (2015) 15](/wiki/Star_Wars_(2015)_15 "Star Wars (2015) 15"), which is set immediately before [*Star Wars* (2015) 20](/wiki/Star_Wars_(2015)_20 "Star Wars (2015) 20"). In these [comics](/wiki/Star_Wars_comic_books "Star Wars comic books"), [Owen Lars](/wiki/Owen_Lars "Owen Lars") is visibly older than his appearance in *[Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi")*, which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of to [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"). Additionally, these comics depict [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") in [Ben Kenobi's home](/wiki/Ben_Kenobi%27s_home "Ben Kenobi's home"), a home he did not occupy until after the events of *Obi-Wan Kenobi*, meaning the comics have to take place after the series. However, [*Star Wars* LINE Webtoon](/wiki/Star_Wars_(LINE_Webtoon) "Star Wars (LINE Webtoon)"): Chapter 2—"Meeting the Droids" depicts Obi-Wan Kenobi visibly older than his appearance in the aforementioned comics; *[Star Wars: The Complete Visual Dictionary, New Edition](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Complete_Visual_Dictionary,_New_Edition "Star Wars: The Complete Visual Dictionary, New Edition")* states that [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") was twelve years old in the Webtoon chapter, and since he was [born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") in 19 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system") according to *Timelines*, he was twelve in [7 BBY](/wiki/7_BBY "7 BBY") and this is the latest the comics can take place. Therefore, due to the year-long gap, *Star Wars* (2015) 7 is set in either 9 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system") or [8 BBY](/wiki/8_BBY "8 BBY"), and *Star Wars* (2015) 15 and *Star Wars* (2015) 20 both take place in either 8 BBY or 7 BBY. 71. [↑](#cite_ref-Hidden_Empire_1_76-0) [*Hidden Empire* 1](/wiki/Hidden_Empire_1 "Hidden Empire 1") 77. ↑ [77.00](#cite_ref-Ghosts_77-0) [77.01](#cite_ref-Ghosts_77-1) [77.02](#cite_ref-Ghosts_77-2) [77.03](#cite_ref-Ghosts_77-3) [77.04](#cite_ref-Ghosts_77-4) [77.05](#cite_ref-Ghosts_77-5) [77.06](#cite_ref-Ghosts_77-6) [77.07](#cite_ref-Ghosts_77-7) [77.08](#cite_ref-Ghosts_77-8) [77.09](#cite_ref-Ghosts_77-9) "[The Ghosts of Maul](/wiki/The_Ghosts_of_Maul "The Ghosts of Maul")" — *[Stories of Jedi and Sith](/wiki/Stories_of_Jedi_and_Sith "Stories of Jedi and Sith")* 78. [↑](#cite_ref-GhostsDate_78-0) *[The Ghosts of Maul](/wiki/The_Ghosts_of_Maul "The Ghosts of Maul")* is set during the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), which *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates the beginning of to 19 BBY. The story also takes place before Maul was stranded on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Malachor](/wiki/Malachor "Malachor"). "[Lightsabers and Jedi Equipment](/wiki/Lightsabers_and_Jedi_Equipment "Lightsabers and Jedi Equipment")" states Maul was stranded [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Mission to Malachor](/wiki/Mission_to_Malachor "Mission to Malachor"), which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates to [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY"). Therefore, he was stranded during or before [5 BBY](/wiki/5_BBY "5 BBY"), and this story must take place sometime between 19 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system") and 5 BBY. 79. Thus, people, even some of the filmmakers, thought it was undecided." ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20190907052642/https://twitter.com/JonKasdan/status/1064690494964416512)) 123. [↑](#cite_ref-Jon's_Tweet_2_123-0) [TwitterLogo](https://twitter.com) [Jon Kasdan](/wiki/Jon_Kasdan "Jon Kasdan") ([@JonKasdan](https://twitter.com/JonKasdan)) on [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "wikipedia:Twitter") ([post](https://twitter.com/JonKasdan/status/1064689594376093701)): "Not exactly true. In the 1st draft, Dryden was second-in-command, a sort of Tom Hagen, to a character called The Kazier, a genial but ruthless Hume Cronyn-type who'd replaced his right-hand w/ a teched-out rococo key. When that character went out, Dryden's superior became Maul." ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20190907052615/https://twitter.com/JonKasdan/status/1064689594376093701)) 124. [↑](#cite_ref-Rule_of_Two_note_132-0) In [*Star Wars*: Episode I *The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") states that there could only be two [Sith Lords](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") at a [time](/wiki/Time "Time"); a [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two") was in place of [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") succession, as explained in the *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* episode "[Sacrifice](/wiki/Sacrifice_(episode) "Sacrifice (episode)")." Since [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") and [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Maul were the two [Dark Lords](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") during *The Phantom Menace*, which *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates to [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"), and that [Darth Plagueis](/wiki/Darth_Plagueis "Darth Plagueis") was Sidious' [Sith Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") according to [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com")'s [Databank](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)"), Plagueis would have have to been the Sith alongside his [apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") before the title of Darth, and hence the mantle of succeeding the remaining place of the Rule of Two, was conferred to Maul, which had been so by the events of *The Phantom Menace*, in 32 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). 133. [↑](#cite_ref-Episode_II_133-0) [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones") |
